League of Nations Executive Council Determines Stance Towards Germany: British and French Attitudes Differ in Flexibility 78

London - After the League of Nations Executive Council formally invited Germany to send a representative, Germany submitted a reply yesterday, accepting the invitation in principle, but with two conditions: 1. The rights enjoyed by the German representative during the Executive Council's discussions and votes should be completely equal to those of other countries' representatives. 2. The resolute stance of France and Belgium, which originally insisted that negotiations on the suggestions in the German memorandum should not begin until German troops withdrew from the Rhineland, must be abandoned. The Executive Council has now responded to this reply, with League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol sending a telegram to Berlin stating, "According to the Locarno Treaty, France and Belgium, like Germany, are guaranteed nations. Therefore, Germany's conditions for participating in the Executive Council's review of the applications from France and Belgium will be the same as those of the two countries. In other words, they have full rights to participate in the discussion, but when voting (to determine the consensus of the Executive Council members), the votes of Germany, France, and Belgium will not be counted. (Note: This means that if the voting results show a consensus among all countries, then regardless of whether Germany, France, or Belgium cast opposing votes, it will be considered a consensus.) As for the guarantee requested by Germany in its second condition, the Executive Council has no authority to grant it to the German government." It is generally understood that British Ambassador to Germany Sir Phipps will engage in further contact with the German Foreign Ministry to facilitate Germany's participation in the Executive Council meeting. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

London - The League of Nations Executive Council held a closed-door meeting at 3:45 PM, chaired by Bruce. He began by reading the German reply. Subsequently, French Foreign Minister Flandin raised several objections to the two German conditions. Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu then proposed that the closed-door meeting be changed to a secret meeting, which the Executive Council decided to do. Therefore, all experts and delegation members, except for the chief representatives of each country, left the venue. Foreign Minister Flandin then continued to express his views, concluding that the first German condition was acceptable, but the second condition was firmly rejected. Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu, Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü, Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov, Polish Foreign Minister Beck, and Spanish Foreign Minister Basilio all spoke, stating that the German conditions could not be accepted. Other national representatives (Great Britain, Argentina, Australia, Portugal, Denmark, Chile, Italy) supported the German view. The meeting then reverted to a closed-door format, ending at 5:20 PM. After two hours, a public meeting was convened, during which French Foreign Minister Flandin presented a joint draft resolution from France and Belgium and made a brief statement beforehand: "The clauses of the Locarno Treaty and Articles 42 and 43 of the Treaty of Versailles have been violated. Our government and our delegation request that the League of Nations Executive Council clearly announce this. The reasons for this have already been explained to the Executive Council, and I do not intend to add anything further. The Belgian government has also authorized me to speak on its behalf. Therefore, I am presenting this joint draft resolution to the Executive Council on behalf of the governments of France and Belgium." Chairman Bruce then read out this draft resolution and stated that due to time constraints, it would be discussed tomorrow. Bruce also read out the Executive Council's reply to Germany. The Executive Council adjourned at 7:40 PM, and a decision was made to hold the next meeting at 3:30 PM tomorrow afternoon. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

London - At the beginning of the public meeting, French Foreign Minister Flandin moved that Germany's military reoccupation of the demilitarized zone in the Rhineland violated Article 43 of the Treaty of Versailles. Belgian Prime Minister van Zeeland seconded the motion. Chairman Bruce then rose and made the aforementioned announcement, and without any discussion, adjourned the meeting until 3:30 PM in the afternoon. At the first closed-door meeting of the Executive Council, Chairman Bruce announced the opening of the meeting. Bruce then asked the representatives whether the subsequent meetings should be held publicly or in private. If held in private, all advisors and secretaries would not be allowed to attend. French Foreign Minister Flandin then rose to speak, criticizing the nature of Germany's reply to the League of Nations' request. Bruce interrupted him due to order concerns. It was then resolved that the Executive Council would hold a secret meeting at 6:00 PM to consider Germany's reply. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

London - The Executive Council held a public meeting for fifteen minutes today and then declared an adjournment until 3:30 PM tomorrow afternoon. Chairman Bruce, the Australian representative, announced that League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol had rejected Germany's conditions for attending the Executive Council meeting. French Foreign Minister Flandin presented a draft resolution to the public meeting to demonstrate France and Belgium's determination to demand sanctions from Britain and Italy. British Foreign Secretary Eden was fiddling with his watch chain, looking very concerned. Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov was relaxed. (National Telegram, 16th)

France and Belgium Submit Draft Resolution to the League of Nations: Condemning Germany for Violating Treaties 79

London - French Foreign Minister Flandin has submitted a joint draft resolution from France and Belgium to the League of Nations Executive Council, which states: "The League of Nations Executive Council, based on the application submitted by France and Belgium on the 8th of this month, hereby resolves as follows: 1. The German government, disregarding the obligations stipulated in Articles 42 and 43 of the Treaty of Versailles and the Locarno Treaty, has sent troops into the demilitarized zone along the Rhine River and stationed them in that area. This action constitutes a violation of Article 43 of the Treaty of Versailles. 2. The Council instructs the Secretary-General to notify the signatory nations of the Locarno Treaty of Germany's violation." (Havas dispatch, 16th)

London - It is generally understood that during today's closed-door meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council, the British representative requested that France and Belgium postpone the submission of their joint draft resolution until the League of Nations received Germany's second reply. However, this proposal was opposed by France. Therefore, the draft resolution was ultimately submitted at the Executive Council's public meeting. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

London - Since Germany abrogated the Locarno Treaty, some have argued that the relevant countries should conclude a new treaty to replace the old one, regardless of whether Germany participates at that time. The representatives of Britain, France, and Belgium immediately submitted separate memoranda to explain the views of their respective governments for presentation at the conference of the Locarno Treaty signatory nations. The Locarno conference was held in private at the Foreign Office this morning at 11:00 AM (originally scheduled to be held at Foreign Secretary Eden's private residence). In addition to Foreign Secretary Eden and Lord Privy Seal Halifax, French Foreign Minister Flandin, Belgian Prime Minister van Zeeland, and Italian Ambassador Grandi also attended. It is reported that the memoranda were discussed. Although the contents of these memoranda have not been disclosed, it is generally understood that the memorandum submitted by France includes three approaches: 1. The Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact should be submitted to the International Court of Justice in The Hague for a ruling to determine whether it conflicts with the Locarno Treaty. 2. The German troops stationed in the Rhineland should be reduced, and its heavy artillery units should be withdrawn to a point 50 kilometers east of the Rhine River. If Germany cannot accept this approach, the relevant countries should immediately decide on economic sanctions. 3. European countries should establish a new security system to replace the Locarno Treaty, so that if the Rhineland cannot be demilitarized, this new security system can provide France with guarantees that are more comprehensive than those originally stipulated in the Locarno Treaty. (Agence Havas dispatch, 17th)

London - It is reported that the Thriteen-Nation Committee will hold a meeting here on Wednesday. French Foreign Minister Flandin will return to Paris to consult with the French cabinet on all matters. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

London - Our diplomatic correspondent has learned that French Foreign Minister Flandin and Minister without Portfolio Penancier plan to return to France this Thursday to report the progress of the diplomatic situation here to the Council of Ministers. It is also said that if the negotiations here can achieve tangible results before the two depart, then future negotiations will continue in Geneva. Furthermore, if Flandin and Penancier do depart, then Belgian Prime Minister van Zeeland also plans to leave here on Wednesday and return to Belgium. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

London - French Foreign Minister Flandin met with Spanish Foreign Minister Basilio, Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov, Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu, and the Yugoslavian Minister to France, Burić, separately this morning for discussions. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

British Cabinet Decides to Continue Mediation Policy: All Locarno Signatories Must Make Concessions 80

London - Regarding Germany's reply to the League of Nations, the British Cabinet held a meeting yesterday and decided to instruct Foreign Secretary Eden to continue the mediation policy. The proposed approach is to demand that each signatory to the Locarno Treaty make some sacrifices in order to reach a peaceful solution. The content of this plan is: 1. Germany must withdraw a portion of its troops stationed in the Rhineland as a sign of good faith. 2. France and Belgium must reduce their hardline attitude towards Germany. In Britain's case, it must fulfill its obligations under the Locarno Treaty and provide military assistance to France and Belgium if they are attacked by Germany in the future. (Havas dispatch, 17th)

London - It is generally understood that at tomorrow's meeting of the Locarno Treaty signatory nations, the British delegation will propose a suggestion to guarantee the security of France and Belgium. When a broader security system is established in the future under the terms of the Locarno Treaty, the measures to guarantee the security of France and Belgium can be incorporated into it. At this time, British officials are still striving for Germany to make concessions and agree to participate in negotiations in order to improve the diplomatic situation, and believe that if Germany can send a representative to the League of Nations Executive Council meeting, it can be considered the first step in making concessions. As for Germany's future representative, Ribbentrop, a confidant of Chancellor Hitler, would be the most suitable. Given the difficult situation, Germany must send a signal of compromise, which Ribbentrop will surely understand. The British Ambassador to Germany will contact the German government again to encourage it to send a representative to the Executive Council meeting. However, the reply issued by the Executive Council today is clearly worded, and any further conditional response from Germany will not be accepted by Britain. It is likely that Germany will request the Executive Council to postpone the meeting so that the German representative can arrive in time. If so, the Executive Council's meeting tomorrow afternoon will inevitably be postponed. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

London - King Edward VIII separately received French Foreign Minister Flandin, Belgian Prime Minister van Zeeland, and Polish Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs Colonel Beck this afternoon. (Havas dispatch, 17th)

Italy-Austria-Hungary: Roman Meeting Postponed; Opens on the 21st 81

Rome - The authorities of Italy, Austria, and Hungary had originally scheduled a meeting to be held here from the 18th to the 20th of this month to strengthen their joint policy based on the Rome Protocols signed by the three countries on March 17th of the year before last. The meeting date has now been changed to the 21st to the 23rd. According to official statements, this meeting has no connection with the events currently being negotiated in London. However, the current international situation is making the future negotiations between Italy, Austria, and Hungary increasingly important, which officials do not deny. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Budapest, Hungary - Prime Minister Gömbös of Hungary was scheduled to depart for Rome tomorrow to attend the meeting of Italy, Austria, and Hungary. Due to the postponement of the meeting, the Prime Minister's departure has also been delayed, and he will likely depart on the 19th, but this is not yet certain. It is reported that the Italian government hopes that Gömbös will postpone his departure until the issue of Germany's entry into the Rhineland has been resolved in London before proceeding. (Havas dispatch, 16th) Italian government and German Embassy spokesmen today both denied that Germany had warned Italy not to participate in League of Nations sanctions against Germany. The London Daily Telegraph previously reported that Germany had warned Italy that its attitude towards the Rhine issue was not friendly and that Germany would stop exporting to Italy, making it unable to resist League of Nations sanctions. Three-Nation Naval Treaty: Drafting Nearing Completion; Anglo-German Negotiations Suspended 83

London - The work of establishing a tripartite naval treaty between Britain, France, and the United States has not stopped its progress due to the international turmoil stirred up by Germany. The work of the small committee responsible for drafting the guarantee clauses is nearing completion. These clauses allow the signatory countries to act contrary to the provisions of the treaty if the shipbuilding of non-signatory countries exceeds the limits stipulated in the treaty. The committee will also draft clauses restricting the use of submarines in wartime. This will be another document. Negotiations between Britain and Germany have been suspended, but this will not delay the signing of the Anglo-French-American naval treaty, which is likely to be signed within the next ten days. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

Japanese Actively Mining Zinc in Northeast China: This Mineral is Highly Needed by Japan; High Quality Receives Exceptional Attention from the Industry 85

Changchun Correspondence: The Manchurian Lead Mine Company, established jointly by South Manchuria Railway and the Japan-Manchuria Mining Company, is currently mining lead and zinc ore at the Yangjiazhai mine. This type of ore is a crucial mineral that is most lacking in Japanese minerals and of very high quality. Therefore, when the ore is sold, the Japanese industry pays exceptional attention to it. Furthermore, when the machines were started at the end of last year, the ore dressing plant could not operate at all due to the temperature. Later, heating was installed to improve the situation, allowing operations to continue. The capacity of the ore dressing is 70 tons per month, and there is an experimental plant capable of processing the raw ore. There are 200 tons of selected ore in storage.

Gansu Province's Hexi Counties Abolish Appropriation System: Provincial Government Orders Immediate Cessation of Payments; Unauthorized Disbursement Will Result in Compensation 86

Lanzhou Correspondence: Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong believes that the appropriation system is riddled with corruption. While Longdong and Longnan have already abolished it, the Hexi counties have not yet done so. Why should there be such a distinction among the people of the same county? Therefore, he resolutely decided to follow the precedent of last year's case and abolish it uniformly from March 1st of this year. As for the issue of military expenses, an agreement has been reached with the New 2nd Army's 100th Division and the 1st Cavalry Division to abolish the appropriation system. The main measures are as follows: 1. No designated appropriations will be made from March 1st onwards. 2. Appropriations that were approved but not yet paid before March 1st will be handled in accordance with the precedent of abolishing military and political appropriations in the 24th and 25th years of the Republic. Payment should be stopped immediately upon receipt of the telegram and the amount stopped should be reported within three days. 3. After the abolition of appropriations, the regular and miscellaneous taxes and land surcharges levied this year should be divided equally and remitted to the provincial treasury monthly without delay. 4. Any long-term appropriations or surcharges used for loans in the past should be handled separately. Unless expressly ordered, this year's tax collections should not be disbursed without authorization to avoid affecting the budget, and any violation will result in compensation. It is reported that the provincial government has clearly instructed and telegraphed the heads of the Hexi counties of Wuwei, Gulang, Linze, Minle, Jinta, Dingxin, Dunhuang, Yongchang, Zhangye, Shandan, Jiuquan, Gaotai, Anxi, and Yumen to comply with these measures. A long-standing corrupt practice has been eliminated in one fell swoop, greatly benefiting the people.

Guangdong Provincial Government Issues Order: People to Serve the Public 87

Provincial Assembly Proposal Passed to Implement Policy Plans to Continue Abolishing Various Harsh Levies Guangzhou Correspondence: At the recent fourth regular meeting of the Guangdong Provincial Assembly, the provincial assemblymen proposed that the people of the province should serve the public to increase the province's production. The proposal was resolved and passed and was sent to the provincial government for handling by the Provincial Assembly. After the provincial government approved the letter, it ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to handle the original proposal. The Department of Civil Affairs, considering this case to be important, should immediately notify all counties to implement it conscientiously, and it has ordered all counties to comply and report to the provincial government for review. The implementation measures are divided into several points: 1. Every able-bodied man in the province should serve the public for one day each month, designating local land reclamation, afforestation, water conservancy, and other public undertakings, which will be directed and supervised by the county and municipal governments and implemented by the district, township, and town offices. If any of these able-bodied men are unable to perform public service due to their duties or work outside the area, they will need to pay a service fee of 1 cent of legal tender per month in lieu of service to the relevant township office, which will be allocated to subsidize the necessary service expenses required to organize local services. 2. Public welfare undertakings should be organized by the counties, starting with the most urgent needs of the locality. The rest should be handled in Egypt. The standard for the most urgent needs of the locality will be resolved by a local villagers' meeting, reported by the district office with its evaluation, and forwarded to the county government for approval. 3. The machinery and medicines required for local people in the counties to serve the public will be proportionally subsidized by the substitution fee for able-bodied men or local public funds, all according to local circumstances. A letter is requested to the provincial government to order the Ministry of Civil Affairs to instruct the counties and cities to comply conscientiously, and the progress of each county and city is to be compiled and submitted to the Ministry for assessment every six months.

In the first three-year policy plan of Guangdong, the abolition of harsh, petty miscellaneous taxes is one of the important tasks. Now that the three-year implementation period has expired, most of the harsh levies in the counties have been abolished. However, there are still a small number of levies that have not been abolished due to the circumstances or insufficient adjustments. Therefore, in the second three-year policy plan, the authorities have decided to abolish all of them, leaving nothing behind. The local budget assessors, who departed yesterday to investigate the counties, and the Ministry of Finance, which sent personnel to inspect the changes in land tax collection in the counties, are all responsible for investigating the status of the harsh, petty miscellaneous levies in the counties. As soon as the Ministry of Finance collects the investigations from the various personnel who have returned to the province, it will formulate a plan to abolish them and include them in the second-stage policy plan for implementation.

Xiamen Prison: Second Escape by Tunneling 88

The tunnel was over a丈 in length, the project was massive, and the mastermind, inmate Su, designed it meticulously.

(Xiamen Correspondence)

Last November, inmates from cell number eight at the Xiamen Court Prison escaped by digging a tunnel. Afterwards, the prison poured a layer of洋灰 (cement) one尺 thick and five尺 wide near the walls of each cell. It was as hard as stone to prevent further digging. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the twelfth of this month at 4:50 AM, during the shift change between Head Guard Xie Baosen and Guards Xie Zhongpin and Xie Shujie, they initially heard inmates in cell number nine chanting Buddhist scriptures very loudly, then suddenly silence. Upon investigating, they found the lower level of the bunk beds had the upper level covered with raised blankets, as if everyone was sound asleep. Feeling something was off, they went to inspect and discovered a deep, dark, immeasurable hole in the ground. When they lifted the raised blankets, they found sacks filled with soil. Greatly alarmed, they raised the alarm.

Military police mobilized and entered the prison to search, while a headcount of the eighteen inmates in cell number nine revealed that nine had escaped. Subsequently, military police captured Lin Zhuang and Zhang Kan, who had not escaped far, nearby. Seven remained at large. As of the evening of the fourteenth, they were still untraced.

The escapees included:

* Su Jianqiu, 26 years old, from Jiangsu, convicted of略誘 (luring away), sentenced to seven years and eight months, plus an additional year and four months for a previous escape.

* Huang Shuizha, 29 years old, from Tong'an, convicted of kidnapping, sentenced to twelve years.

* Wu Ben, from Tong'an, 30 years old, convicted of murder, sentenced to ten years.

* Wu Qi, 23 years old, from Guangdong, convicted of robbery, sentenced to one year and six months.

* Lin Zhu, 20 years old, from Jinmen, convicted of murder, sentenced to life imprisonment, appeal pending.

* Xie Derun, 35 years old, from Tong'an, convicted of robbery, sentenced to ten years.

* Lin Pengfei, 18 years old, from Nan'an, convicted of robbery, sentenced to five years.

An inspection by the court revealed that the opening of the tunnel was only one尺 eight寸 long, one尺 three寸 wide, and three尺 deep, located about five尺 from the wall, precisely at the edge of the洋灰 (cement) flooring. After removing two bricks, they dug down to a depth of three尺 eight寸, then turned horizontally to form a secret passage. It extended seven尺 outside the wall of cell number nine, then four尺 through a passageway by the women's prison, reaching the side of Jiangcuo Lane outside the prison wall. The tunnel was one丈 two or three尺 long, one尺 seven寸 high, and one尺 three寸 wide, only allowing one person to crawl through. The exit was one尺 eight寸 long and one尺 four寸 wide.

Questioning the captured Lin and Zhang, they confessed that Su Jianqiu was the mastermind. Su was originally sentenced to seven years. He escaped once two years ago, was caught, and had his sentence increased by eight months. Last year, he escaped again, was caught, and had his sentence increased by another year and four months. This was his thirteenth attempt. The digging tool was only a small wooden stick, about a尺 long. It had taken a long time to dig. A mouthwash cup was found in the tunnel, containing flour and oil mixed with a little soot. At night, they quietly dug, and during the day, they covered the bricks, using the mixture to seal and smooth the brick seams to make them look normal, avoiding the guards' attention. The excavated soil was placed in broken bedding and old clothes torn and sewn into bags. During the day, they were kept inside the tunnel, unnoticed, and at night, they were taken out for work. This went on for several days. On the day they completed the tunnel and escaped, they distributed the soil bags on the beds of the escapees and covered them with blankets, creating the illusion of sound sleepers. Later, over sixty bags of soil were discovered, revealing the magnitude of the project and the length of time it took. The nine inmates who did not escape all claimed ignorance. Cell number nine was directly adjacent to cell number eight. Less than four months apart, two separate tunneling escapes occurred. Head Guard Xie Maisen and the other two guards were all detained.

Furthermore, Su Jianqiu, having escaped twice before, was originally under close observation by the guards. Recently, Su had suddenly changed his behavior, strongly expressing remorse and encouraging fellow inmates to do good deeds and chant Buddhist scriptures together. As a result, the guards viewed him favorably and did not suspect ulterior motives. Two matchboxes were found in the tunnel, connected by over a丈 of white silk, used for communication within the tunnel, like a telephone. The depth of his planning is evident.

(March 15th)

Going to Ta'er Monastery

West Post Correspondence

Travelogue of Qinghai (Continued): Ta'er Monastery Lamp Festival 89

On the ninth day of the second lunar month, we left the interesting Sangsige and followed the Hongyazi Gorge down. After passing the Lower Village, twenty li away, we arrived at a Han Chinese village and spent the night at Gao Village, located on the road to Xining. According to local Han Chinese tradition, their ancestors were exiled from Nanjing Zhuzixiang during the Six Dynasties. Their pronunciation of "I" as "nu" sounds very similar to the dialect of Songjiang Prefecture.

The next day, we arrived in Xining early. We were graciously hosted by Commander Ma Bufang and stayed at the Kunlun Hotel for four consecutive days. On the morning of the tenth day of the lunar month, he sent a car, along with Director Wang and Secretary Wang, to take Director Zhang Xiguang, representative of Chairman Yu of Gansu, and us to Ta'er Monastery to see the Lantern Festival.

Ta'er Monastery is ninety li south of Xining. The car exited the south gate and struggled several times on the frozen river. After repairs, it drove onto the main road. People rushing to the festival were everywhere, a colorful and endless stream. Some were riding horses, others were in轿車 (sedan cars). The car sped forward, raising a cloud of dust. Many Tibetan horses, having never seen a car, broke free from their tethers and ran away. The horse ran ahead, the car drove behind, the horse thinking it was a wild beast trying to eat it, running away in panic. Several village dogs frantically chased the car, barking as they ran, as if racing against the car.

After fifty li, the car passed through the bustling town of Lusha, drove up a hillside, and the snowy white tents filled the valleys. The sound of trumpets dispersed the crowds. The car stopped in front of Ta'er Monastery, which was 2800 meters above sea level. A lama guided us to rest in a僧房 (monk's cell) behind the "Little Golden Tile Temple."

Impression of Meeting the Panchen Lama

Since it was still early, we followed the guiding lama to visit the Panchen Lama. The Lama's 行轅 (official residence) was located in the red walls shimmering across the street. We went up the hillside, crowded with red-robed lamas because he was to receive the worship of 3,500 lamas from Ta'er Monastery today and the worship of the people tomorrow. Since he had not yet come out of the palace, we followed the guiding lama into the gate. A yellow satin 法座 (throne) was already set up in the center of the courtyard.

Several red-hatted堪布 (abbots) came out to greet us and took us to the secretariat. We were all embarrassed because we had prepared to pay homage to the Lama but had not brought a哈達 (ceremonial scarf), the Tibetan greeting gift. In the end, we could only offer our name cards. After waiting a long time, we chatted with his entourage and learned that the Lama was scheduled to go to Labrang Monastery (Xiahe County, Gansu) at the end of the second lunar month and would return to Tibet via Yushu and Derge in April or May.

A translator wearing a purple-red robe came down and said "Please." A total of nine of us followed him through the courtyard, up a short flight of stairs, and into a dimly lit禅房 (meditation room). A master in a袈裟 (robe), with a wizened face, a beard, and a benevolent expression, came out to greet us. We bowed in the Han Chinese manner, and he very politely gave each of us a cyan-gray哈達 (ceremonial scarf), and greeted us in broken Chinese, "Please sit," "Please sit." Afterwards, through the translator, we offered our respects and exchanged pleasantries. Because he was in a hurry to leave, we could not discuss his return to Tibet. As we parted, he shook hands with everyone. At this time, I noticed that his face was much thinner than when we met in Nanjing the year before, probably due to his worries about the country and the times.

Paying Respects at the Holy Mausoleum

Walking out of the 行轅 (official residence) gate, the golden tiles on the roof of the "Great Golden Tile Temple" shone towards me. It is commonly said that its value is equivalent to the庚子賠款 (Boxer Rebellion Indemnity), so we paid close attention. The roof was divided into two layers, in the style of a palace, surrounded by a cloth curtain with a six-character mantra. In the center of the ridge, there were three golden domes. The beautiful tiles reflected an unbearable yellow light towards the audience. As for whether it was pure gold or gilded, we had no time to investigate further.

At the foot of the temple walls, crowds of Mongolian and Tibetan people were prostrating themselves, competing to measure the circumference of the temple with their bodies. Next to it was a revolving scripture house, a row of "嘛呢輪" (prayer wheels) spinning non-stop. The people pushing the wheels were packed so tightly that there was no space, sometimes even two people pushing one axle at the same time.

The lama led us into the temple to pay respects at the "Holy Mausoleum"! The floor was worn into very deep grooves by the heads of the Buddhist believers. Opening the gate, we entered the solemn and majestic hall, which houses the body of宗喀巴 (Tsongkhapa), the founder of the "Yellow Sect." Therefore, the Great Golden Tile Temple has unparalleled value in Lamaism. The light in the Holy Mausoleum was exceptionally dim. In the light of the butter lamps, we saw a tall pagoda, the four walls of which were covered with delicate and beautiful神帳 (divine curtains) and佛　(Buddhist images).

To the left of the temple exit, there was a withered tree surrounded by a wooden fence, its branches scattered. The lama pointed and said, "宗喀巴 (Tsongkhapa)'s" placenta is buried here, so this bodhi tree grew. At the same time, we found several yellow Tibetan letters on a new branch, their strokes resembling wormholes. These are mostly the灵迹 (miraculous traces) of 宗喀巴 (Tsongkhapa). Several devout Tibetan women touched their heads to the wooden fence to show their respect.

Kunshan Jiancha Shi, Ding Chaowu, Arrives in Kunshan for Inspection

Jiangsu Inspector Ding Chaowu arrived in Kunshan from Shanghai on the morning of the sixteenth. After getting off the train, he drove directly to the county government to meet County Magistrate Peng. He inquired in detail about the county's administrative facilities. He then attended the joint memorial week speech. He said that all counties must focus on production and construction to solve the people's livelihood problems. In the afternoon, he went to various agencies for detailed inspections. He is expected to stay for one or two days.

A Jiangbei Woman Dies Tragically Under Train Wheels

A Jiangbei woman, about forty years old, a resident east of the railway洋橋 (foreign bridge) in Zhengyi Shiliting, a suburb of the county, was walking along the railway tracks on the evening of the previous day when a third- or fourth-class Shanghai-Nanjing train sped by. The woman was unable to avoid it in time and was knocked down, her thigh severed. She died on the spot, her flesh and blood blurred, a tragic sight. The driver, realizing he had caused the accident, stopped the train and dragged the body to the side of the tracks. He then drove to Zhengyi Station and informed the stationmaster to prepare a coffin for burial.

Suzhou Policemen Murder Case Appeal Opens

The case of He Naikang, a patrolman from the fifth precinct of the first public security bureau; Hong Shiqin, a patrol officer; Xu Baosheng, a patrol chief; Zhou Fan Qian Shugang; and four others conspiring to murder Gu Agen, a incense man from the Chen family nunnery at No. 46 Guanzai Lane, had its first hearing in the Jiangsu High Court yesterday (17th). The Wu County District Court originally sentenced He Naikang to death and Hong Shiqin to ten years in prison, with the other defendants also receiving separate sentences. The defendants refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. In addition to summoning the detained defendants, the court also subpoenaed Yan Jishi, the Chief Inspector of the Public Security Bureau, Xue Yijun, the Detective Captain of the Detective Team, and witnesses Cao Xiangshi and others. He Naikang hired lawyer Yao Xiaoqiu, Hong Shiqin hired lawyer Zhu Fucheng, and Xu Baosheng hired lawyer Jin Henian to defend them separately. At 10:30 am, Judge Siwen took the stand in the first criminal court to hear the case. He Naikang and others adamantly denied conspiring to murder Gu Agen. Because the case was complex, the interrogation lasted for five hours before the court adjourned. He Naikang and others were returned to custody, and subpoenas will be issued to witnesses for another scheduled court hearing. In addition, He Naikang's mother, He Zhou, published a large number of grievances yesterday (17th), defending her son on the grounds that he was falsely accused of murder and wrongly sentenced.

Wuxi Qu Shus Large Petition

The county government of this county recently approved a letter from the county party department to abolish the district book collection fee in order to reduce the burden on the people. After learning of this, the bookers believed that if the collection of books were abolished while their duties remained the same, their livelihoods would be at risk. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, they elected petition representatives Shi Shouxuan, Wang Hanchen, Zhang Gongmei, Mao Fengming and other representatives. Ten people led more than 400 district officials to the county party department to petition for relief. Gao Zugao received them and promised to forward the letter to the county government for review. Then, they went to the county government to petition. Section Chief Huang received them and relayed to the representatives that the district officials will be allowed to continue under the old system until the land survey is completed and the district officials' positions are not abolished. The representatives were satisfied and withdrew.

Changzhou Murderer Who Strangled His Nephew Sentenced to Death

Tan Guangyu, a villager from the Nanmin Weixiang township in the third district of Wu County, was strangled by his uncles, Tan Falong and Tan Faming, for fighting over inheritance. During a night patrol last winter, they strangled Guangyu and threw his body into the river. The body was later recovered, and the murderers, Tan Falong and Tan Faming, were arrested and sent to the District Court Procuratorate for investigation. After repeated investigations, the debate was declared closed and the sentencing was scheduled for the 16th. The main text stated that Tan Falong was sentenced to death for the crime of joint murder, and Tan Faming was sentenced to life imprisonment.

Zhenjiang National Goods Year Opening Ceremony Scheduled.

The Jiangsu National Goods Year opening ceremony will be held in the Provincial Party Department Auditorium at 9:00 a.m. on the 25th of this month. At the same time, a parade will be held at the Provincial Public Stadium, and a lantern parade will be held in the evening. The National Goods Cigarette Association will gather cigarette companies to customize lanterns that fit the names of cigarettes to participate in the parade, and will rehearse on the evening of the 24th, preparing a large number of exotic fireworks to be set off in the stadium.

The Jiangsu Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee, because the local budgets of each county in this province for the 25th year have been successively compiled and sent to the province, previously sent a letter to the Ministry of Finance, proposing to order the hall to participate in the review, and the Ministry of Finance has approved it. It is now known that the Financial Hall has received the Ministry's order and expressed its welcome, because it will be helpful in abolishing excessive taxes and reducing surcharges, and has written to the Association to immediately send members to participate in the review. At the same time, the compensation money for the four batches of excessive taxes abolished can also be discussed together.

Gaoyou Bandits Rampant, Two Robberies

Bandits have been rampant in this county recently, and robbery cases have occurred repeatedly. There have now been two robbery cases, described as follows:

* At 2:00 a.m. yesterday (12th), eight bandits, each carrying guns, swords, broke into the home of Qiu Changxiao, a villager in the Qili township in the fifth district. The family members were awakened from their dreams. The bandits first tied up Geng Yong with ropes, then robbed 51 yuan in silver dollars and clothes and other items from the boxes in the room, before leaving. Geng has reported to the county government, requesting a strict investigation of the bandits.

* Around 10:00 p.m. the other day, two bandit ships, carrying more than a dozen bandits armed with guns, came to the home of Lu Chenzhi and Wang Longkou in Donggou, Gonghu township, in the second district. The bandits searched the Wang family for a long time, but found no silver dollars, only stealing clothes and jewelry worth more than 100 yuan. When the bandits left, one of them fell behind. Wang immediately invited neighbors to pursue them. The bandit then fired a shot, hitting neighbor Xu Er's head. Wang and others dared not pursue them further, and the bandit was able to escape leisurely.

Nantong Clearing District's Accumulated Opium Cases

The cases of trafficking opium in the counties of Tong, Ru, Hai, Chong, Qi, and Jing under the Nantong District Hall are all under the jurisdiction of the Commissioner's Office Military Law Office for trial. Because the counties are constantly sending prisoners, there are many accumulated cases, and the male and female prisoners in the detention center are extremely crowded. Commissioner Ge is implementing a clearance, and Military Law Officer Zhu Feiru is expediting the resolution. Once a case is closed, it will be returned to the original county for execution.

Strange Kidnapping and Arson

Ge Jinfeng, a girl from Guanyin Mountain, was betrothed to Qian Lifan. Recently, something changed. The Qian family then gathered a crowd to kidnap the bride and hid the Ge girl in Cheng Rongshou's house. The Ge family then invited relatives and friends, such as Luo Huiyi, to Cheng's house in an attempt to snatch her back. Because they could not find her, they set fire to the house, hoping that the Ge girl would run out so that they could snatch her back, but they still did not see her. Cheng Rongshou accused Luo Huiyi. The court opened the trial on the 14th, and Luo and others were released on bail.

Guard Accidentally Kills Merchant

Mao Ganru, the班長 (squad leader) of the Yushu Baochang guard post, led his patrol officers on patrol at midnight. They went to Zhang's tofu shop to eat tofu soup. The rifle of guard Shi Fengfei accidentally discharged, and the bullet entered the adjacent Li Tongmao store. The shop owner was settling accounts, and the bullet hit a vital point, killing him on the spot. Shi Fengfei was taken into custody by the court.

Hangzhou Haimen Pond Presents a Dangerous Situation

Near Guanyintang in the North River of Hangzhou City, the soil embankment was destroyed by the surge of the Qiantang River spring tide, and the farmland was flooded, which was very dangerous. Zhou Zhenlun, Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, went to investigate in person on the afternoon of the 17th, intending to ask the city government to allocate money to build a dam for defense. Also, the Tangjiao of the Hangping Section Bingzi Haimen Pond was destroyed by the water, and cracks were found in the Tangjiao. The Water Conservancy Bureau has rushed to repair it. Also, the Duzi Tang body is tilted outward, and the Tangjiao is empty, which is extremely dangerous. The Water Conservancy Bureau specially telegraphed the Construction Department to allocate money for repairs.

Central Savings Association Establishes Branch

The Central Savings Association opened in Shanghai on the 16th. Hangzhou has decided to set up a branch and has appointed Zhang Shaofu as the director, responsible for preparations. The address is located at the original site of the Wanguo Savings Association in Chenchang Money Shop in Zhubao Lane. It is expected to open on the 24th of this month. There are many depositors of the Chinese and French Savings Association in Hangzhou, who will all be transferred to the Association.

City Government Takes Over West Lake Auditorium

The former West Lake Expo West Lake Auditorium building has been approved by the provincial government and transferred to the city government for use as a group wedding hall and public meeting place. Yesterday, the two parties appointed personnel to handle the transfer procedures. All equipment and fifteen city houses on the Xiling Bridge were taken over and managed by the Hangzhou City Government.

Travelogue of Han and Yue (7) 90

— Zhao Junhao

(Travel Correspondence from Our Reporter)

From Hengyang to Chenzhou Pingshi

On the morning of the eighth, I and others took the Zhushao Railway Engineering Automobile from Hengyang and headed towards Laiyang and Chenzhou, with Pingshi as the destination. Zhou Xia and Nie, three engineering inspectors from the Ministry of Railways, traveled with us. They were all going to Chenzhou to supervise the construction. The road from Hengyang to Chenzhou has already been opened to traffic, but the train runs slowly because the track is newly built. It will take until dusk to reach Chenzhou. According to our planned itinerary, we had to reach Pingshi today, so we continued to advance along the Xiang Province Highway in the engineering automobile. After departing from Bai Hengyang, the land gradually moved south, the climate became warmer, and the sky was clear today, making the car very comfortable. On the way, we sometimes saw the railway line crossing the highway. The highway can be bent according to the terrain, while the railway focuses on cutting off bays and taking shortcuts, so it cannot be too curved. The car passed Laiyang without stopping and continued to advance, arriving in Chenzhou at noon.

Bangzhou is a large city in southern Hunan. Because it is close to Guangdong Province, with overlapping peaks and mountains, the area is known for its instability. The communists Zhu and Mao first launched their uprising here. Li Zongbao, who has now returned to the Central Government, was very famous in the Red Army, and is said to be from Chenzhou. After getting off the car at the highway station, we first went to the Fourth Engineering Section of the Zhushao Railway Bureau to meet Chief Engineer Liu Baoshan. The three Ministry of Railways inspectors were temporarily stationed here. After lunch in the section, we were led by engineer Tan Yi to visit the historical sites of Chenzhou, which have great value. There is the Three Perfections Stele, with lyrics by Qin Shaoyou, paintings by Mi Nangong, and carvings by Su Ziyou. It is called the Three Perfections, but the text on the stele is too worn, and it is difficult to identify without careful examination and reference to ancient books. Mr. Tan said that he is on good terms with a principal of a Chenzhou middle school, and learned the original text from him, and eagerly copied it as follows:

Mist loses the terraces, the moon confuses the ferry, where can we hope to reach Peach Blossom Spring? How can one endure the cold of spring in this lonely inn, amid the rhododendrons and the setting sun?

Postal service sends plum blossoms, fish deliver letters, layer upon layer of regrets are accumulated. Chen River originally circles Chen Mountain, for whom does it flow down to Xiaoxiang?

In addition, there is the Su Xian Pavilion, the story of which is detailed in Ancient and Modern Wonders. Roughly, it is said that Su Dan's mother conceived because she was touched by a fairy, and gave birth to Dan. After Dan grew up, he rode a crane to become an immortal. To this day, there is a fairy stone on the pavilion, with the claw marks of the crane still on the stone. There is also the Orange Well Temple. It is said that Su Dan's mother left a message before her death that Chenzhou would definitely have a major epidemic next year. If the orange leaves are taken from the water in the well and drunk, it can be resolved. Later, her words were verified. The site of the well still exists today, and the word "Orange Well" commonly used by doctors originated from this, it is said. In addition to the above, there is also the Tomb of Emperor Yi, a story of Han Gaozu and Xiang Yu. The Yi Fish Pavilion is a story of Han Yu passing through Chenzhou on his southern exile. All of the above are mostly myths, but it goes without saying that Chenzhou has a long history. The Chen County Government cooperates well with the railway, and even asked the engineering section to plan roads for the local area, one built along the mountains, and one running through the urban area, which is connected to the Chenzi Highway. Everything is now in full swing.

Chenzhou also has a hot spring, six huai away from the station. Because we still had time, we asked Mr. Tan to guide us on a tour of the hot spring. It is said that this spring was discovered by Tan Yanyue, and he bathed here when he was in Changsha. We still took a car for 20 minutes, and then walked for 20 minutes to reach the spring. The spring is at the foot of a small mountain, bubbling endlessly all year round. The water is slightly warm and rich in minerals. However, the facilities are very simple. The bath pool is square and open-air, with a tile roof and short walls around it. When we arrived, there were more than a dozen villagers naked, pounding bricks, which was very unsightly. After the patrol police persuaded them to leave, we were able to see the pool in detail. There is probably only one spring stream, but the water is very strong. I tried to explore it with my hand, and the water temperature seemed to be similar to the Tangshan hot spring in Nanjing. The road bureau is now planning to open a road from the station to here. The surrounding trees are lush and the environment is not bad. If we add management and set up exquisite bathtubs, Chenzhou, with this hot spring and the above-mentioned attractions, will surely attract many tourists.

After visiting the hot spring, we continued to move forward in the original car. At this time, the car was driving on the mountain, and the slope was very steep. Because the border between Hunan and Guangdong has many mountains, the highway follows the mountain trend. At 4:00 p.m., we passed Yizhang and saw a avenue by the roadside. We stopped the car to watch. The avenue was very wide, and all of the stone panels are neatly paved, with rows of ancient pine trees on both sides. The branches and leaves are green and lush, and it is endless. It is impossible to plant these ancient pine trees in less than one or two hundred years. The most amazing thing is that this method of planting trees and paving roads is no different from modern urban design, which shows that the civilization of ancient Chinese architecture is worthy of our admiration. The driver said that this avenue is called Chenzhou Avenue, and it can go directly from Chenzhou to Yizhang, but the history of the avenue still needs to be investigated, and there is nothing to write about in the journey. From this all the way down, the scenery is better and better. There are countless numbers of people carrying salt to the north on the way, no less than several hundred people, all of whom are selling salt from Guangdong Province to Hunan. The car went further, and after passing Xiaotang Station, it was the boundary of Guangdong Province. The highway in Guangdong Province is extremely steep, and the road turns with the mountains, circling back and forth, forming a large loop. The car was driving almost on the top of the mountain. Looking down to the left and right, the small mountains were all under our feet. If the driver had not handled it properly, there would have been many dangers. After entering Guangdong, we soon arrived at Pingshi, where the Third Engineering Section of the Zhushao Railway Bureau is located. The office buildings are built on small hills, and the green peaks are in pieces from a distance. The scenery is extremely beautiful and natural. That night, we stayed in the engineering section.

Local News

Ambassador Liu's Observations: A Major European War Unlikely to Erupt 91

According to the Central News Agency, China's Ambassador to Italy, Liu Wendao, traveled to Hangzhou on the 15th and then to Moganshan to visit Huang Yingbai. That evening, he came to Shanghai to proceed to Nanjing, where he successively met with Chairman Lin, President Chiang, and Foreign Minister Zhang. He also attended the Central Memorial Week. On the afternoon of the 16th, at 5 PM, he left Nanjing to return to Shanghai, arriving here around 10:30 PM that night and going directly to his private residence on Haig Road to rest. On the evening of the 17th, at 7 PM, he hosted a banquet at his private residence for the Italian Ambassador to China, Aloisi, the Consul General in Shanghai, Nielong, and senior officials from the embassy and consulate. Liu had originally planned to go to Hangzhou on the 19th at the invitation of the Central Aviation School to give a lecture on international issues, returning to Shanghai that evening or the next morning. On the 20th, he was to attend a banquet hosted by Mayor Wu. On the 22nd, he would take a night train to Nanjing to meet with Chairman Lin, President Chiang, and Foreign Minister Zhang again to receive further instructions and bid farewell. After a one-day stay in Nanjing, he would return to Shanghai. On the 24th, he would attend a banquet on the Italian mail ship Victoria, and on the 26th, he would board the Victoria to return to his post in Italy. Mrs. Liu decided to postpone her departure for a few months due to her recent childbirth. As for the newly appointed Counselor of the Chinese Embassy in Italy, Shen Zutong, who had originally planned to accompany Liu on the same ship, he also decided to postpone his departure until the 24th of next month, when he will travel with his family on the Italian mail ship Conte Verde, due to some private matters at home. Shen flew from Nanjing to Xi'an on the 17th to meet with Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang and returned to Nanjing on the 19th to await Liu's audience. When a reporter visited Liu on the morning of the 17th to inquire about the developments in the European situation, Liu declined to comment, only saying that the European countries deeply felt the pain of the European War and were unwilling to rekindle the flames of war. Furthermore, the current opposing fronts in Europe are not clear, and the strength is not balanced. Therefore, in his observation, the possibility of a second major war breaking out is more than 90%. As for his decision to go to Hangzhou to visit Huang Yingbai, it was because they had not met for many years, so he made a special trip to reminisce about old times, and there were absolutely no other missions.

Shanghai Bank Note Exchange Foundation First Set at Ten Million Yuan, Acceptance to Begin After Price Evaluation is Approved 94

According to New Voice News Agency, after the establishment of the Shanghai Bank Note Exchange, the exchange foundation, according to Article 2 of the regulations, will be subscribed by the member banks. The banks that have been approved for the foundation are the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Corporation, Shanghai Salt Industry Bank, Jin Cheng Bank, Dalu Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Guohuo Bank, Guohua Bank, Zhongfu Bank, Industry Bank, China Industrial Bank, Siming Bank, Exchange Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Xinhua Bank, Wing Hang Bank, China Bank, China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Tonghe Bank, Juxingcheng Bank, Zhonghui Bank, Quanye Bank, Enterprise Bank, Silk Industry Bank, Women's Bank, Zhejiang Local Bank, Sichuan Meifeng Bank, Jiangsu Farmers Bank, Yongda Bank, Hengli Bank, and the Four Banks Savings Association, Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, a total of 35 banks. The total amount is 10 million yuan in national currency.

Establishment of an Agreement

The exchange decided to wait until the operation is effective before expanding further. The total amount of the foundation will also be increased at any time as needed. All banks that join as members of the exchange will sign an agreement and, in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the regulations, bear their responsibility according to the percentage of the total amount occupied by the amount of note acceptance foundation they subscribe to. Currently, member banks have submitted the types of collateral stipulated in Article 18 of the regulations to the exchange for acceptance. It has been decided to sign the acceptance after the evaluation team evaluates the discount and the committee approves it. The deadline is at most 90 days.

Publication of Interest Rates

Bank-accepted notes can be circulated, bought, sold, and discounted on the market. If necessary, they can apply to the exchange for rediscount. The exchange publishes the discount rate daily and can also apply to the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications for rediscount. The matters concerning rediscount have been properly negotiated by the chairman and manager of the exchange, Zhu Boquan, with the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. The credit of these accepted notes is very good, and all banks and firms are happy to receive them.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Advocates Commercial Rectification Movement 95

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, upon receiving a letter from the Shanghai Silk Industry Association, stated that Huahua Silk Company proposed that businesses in the same industry cut prices and compete for sales and use false advertising to deceive customers, requesting that measures be taken to ban such practices. The City Chamber of Commerce believes that this kind of false competition is rampant in the market. In recent months, the Chamber has also frequently received letters from customers in other cities entrusting the Chamber to inquire about cases of receiving money but not shipping goods, and false low prices. The Chamber believes that this kind of loss of commercial ethics should be strictly rectified. Yesterday, it specifically issued a notice to merchants and submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry to stipulate penalties to maintain commercial regulations. The original text is recorded as follows:

Notice to Merchants

To all store managers and supervisors in the city: The morality of Chinese merchants has always been respected by both domestic and foreign parties. Therefore, "genuine goods at fair prices" and "no deception of the old or young" have been popular terms in the business world for hundreds of years. In recent years, the market has been sluggish, and business has become increasingly difficult. Therefore, each store, in order to struggle for survival, invariably does not hesitate to use all extraordinary means in order to attract customers. There are so-called "buy one get one free," "buy one get two free," and even, according to the report of the Silk Industry Association, advertised sales of fine satin at a price of one cent per foot. Consider that merchants seek profit from capital, and at least they must preserve their capital. Such behavior that harms others and does not benefit oneself is not only a public enemy to the same industry, but also inevitably artificial and deceptive to customers. Although some customers who are greedy for small gains may be used by them, they can only deceive for a while. Over time, the public will spread rumors, the tricks will be exposed, and in the end, no one will ask about them. Therefore, wanting to rely on these extraordinary means to maintain and develop business is tantamount to abandoning a smooth road and heading towards a dead end. Since ancient times, the success of a merchant's career has no other secret. It is nothing more than encouraging oneself with caution and diligence, treating others with fairness and clarity, treating customers with humility, and treating the same industry with mutual assistance. If the above principles are abandoned and new patterns are desired, there is no one who will not stumble and fall. This Chamber, as the leader of the city's business community, shares the same fate and speaks with sincerity. From now on, correct mistakes if there are any, and strive harder if there are none. This notice.

Document Submitted to the Ministry of Industry

Submitted for the matter of submitting a request, (excerpt) It has been found that stores use fraudulent methods to attract customers or use improper means to undermine each other. Your Ministry issued instruction number 40287, ordering the City Social Affairs Bureau to ban and punish such practices, and the industry rules established by various industries in the city and filed with the competent authorities also have similar public restrictions. Those who violate the rules may have the trade association formulate penalty measures and submit them to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval and execution. However, the commercial center of this city is located in the concessions. The Social Affairs Bureau's decision to ban and punish those who violate industry rules is difficult to implement due to the limitations of the established international situation. Therefore, Your Ministry's instruction number 40287 and the current request of the trade association are consistent in substance. However, the difficulty lies in how to eliminate the obstacles to banning and punishing. It has been found that in the concessions, the execution of administrative penalties is mostly entrusted to the Special District Court. For example, in the case of stamp tax violations, when the mainland was still organizing a violation case hearing committee under the tax bureau to hear and punish the case, the concessions first handled it through the Special District Court. This is because the administrative power in the concessions is limited, and there is no way to provide relief except in this way. In the future, in the case of violations of industry rules in the concessions, if we can follow the stamp tax precedent and change the hearing and punishment to be executed by the Special District Court, it concerns the maintenance of the entire commercial regulations. It is appropriate to prepare a document and request your Ministry to examine, approve, and instruct to comply. This is truly in the public interest.

Reply to the Silk Industry

Replying directly, we received your association's letter regarding the matter of various industries using dishonest means to entice customers, requesting that the government investigate and ban such practices and notify various industries to stop them. We have noted the details. It has been found that these malpractices are prohibited in the industry rules that have been submitted and approved by various industries. All trade associations are deeply distressed by this matter. Moreover, the Ministry of Industry's instruction number 40287 also ordered the Social Affairs Bureau to strictly ban and punish such practices, and those who violate industry rules may formulate penalty measures and submit them to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval and execution. However, the most difficult point in this case is that the shops opened in the concessions, whether they are members of the trade association or not, are bound by the established international situation, and the Social Affairs Bureau cannot exercise its power to ban and punish them. Today, in order to eliminate obstacles, we should start from this point. This Chamber has already submitted a separate document to the Ministry of Industry based on your association's letter to plan effective measures. On the other hand, it has also issued a notice to merchants in order to encourage mutual vigilance. It is appropriate to reply and request your attention.

Mr. Fritz's Lecture: Modern Long-Distance Telephone 97

According to a National News Agency dispatch from Shanghai on the 17th, the China Branch of the Institute of Electrical Engineers held an academic lecture yesterday afternoon at the Lester Institute of Technology. Mr. Fritz was specially invited to lecture on "Modern Long-Distance Telephone." The audience included members of the Chinese Institute of Engineers. Mr. Fritz said that although various problems related to long-distance telephone have been studied in electrical engineering laboratories for more than 50 years, there was no significant progress until between 1912 and 1915. After the European War, the United Kingdom and the European continent began to conduct considerable experiments. In terms of international aspects, after the President of the Institute of Electrical Engineers, Mr. Gill (Mr. Gill also resided in Shanghai), called attention to long-distance telephone in his inaugural speech, Europe officially began to plan the development of long-distance telephone lines. Later, the International Telephone Discussion Committee was established in Paris, which also made considerable contributions to long-distance telephone. In the past 15 years, the world has invested no less than 30 million pounds in long-distance telephone. The telephone networks between European countries are expanding day by day. In 1927, the scope of long-distance telephone was expanded with wireless electricity. Initially, there was communication between Europe and the United States, and the progress was very rapid. It has changed from long wave to short wave. In 1928, passengers in boats and vehicles were able to enjoy the convenience of telephone. Transatlantic mail ships can communicate with London, New York, and various places on the mainland. Now China has a network covering nine provinces, and plans have been made for future expansion. A line between Shanghai and Guangzhou is being laid. The most difficult problems in telephone engineering are echoes, distortion, and noise. Now there are considerable solutions. Today, there are 33 million telephone users worldwide. The hope of Shanghai communicating with the farthest places in the world is not far away. In short, the task of telephone engineers is to reduce engineering costs and increase efficiency, because long-distance telephone is really necessary for the business community and the convenience of the public, and it is not just a luxury for the rich.

There Was a Gale in the City Yesterday, Memorial Meeting Held at the Lake Society at 2 PM, Party and Government Agencies Sent Representatives to Attend and Guide 99

According to the Central News Agency, yesterday was the March 17th National Doctors' Day. Various Chinese medicine and Chinese medicine organizations in the city held a memorial meeting at 2 PM yesterday in the auditorium of the Lake Society. The meeting place was decorated extremely simply and solemnly. No less than a thousand people from all walks of life and the Chinese medicine community attended. Party and government agencies sent representatives to attend and guide. The meeting adjourned at 4 PM. The details are recorded as follows: Those who attended included Mao Xiaxuan from the City Party Headquarters, Wu Liguo from the Municipal Government, Zhong Zhiqi from the Health Bureau, Nie Haifan from the Education Bureau, Mao Shenghe from the Social Affairs Bureau, Lin Kanghou from the National Federation of Commerce (represented by Tao Leqin), Ding Zhongying from the Shanghai Branch of the Central National Medical Museum (represented by Ye Jinqiu), Zhu Shoupeng from the National Medicine Chunqiu Society, Ding Boan from the Guangyi Shantang, Shen Shenxiu from the Kunshan Chinese Medicine Association, and all members of the Shanghai Chinese Medicine Association, Shanghai Chinese Medical Society, Chinese National Medical Society, Shenzhou National Medical Society, and the Shanghai Chinese Pharmaceutical Industry Trade Union, as well as all teachers and students from the Chinese Medicine College and the China Medical College, totaling more than a thousand people.

Meeting Staff

Presidium: Xie Liheng, Xia Yingtang, Guo Boliang, Gu Weichuan, Ding Jiwan, Gao Zhiwen; Secretaries: Zhang Zanchen, Xu Ziming, Cheng Diren, Yu Tongfang, Fei Yongzuo; Master of Ceremonies: Huang Peisheng; Accountant: Xiao Tuian; Directors: Xue Wenyuan, Ding Zhongying, Qin Bowei, Shi Jiqun, Pan Yusheng, Bao Juxiang, Guo Zhongliang, Sheng Weizhou, Hong Juqing, He Yunsheng, Yu Hongsun, Song Furen, Shen Hefu, Qiu Yanling; Disciplinarians: All executive and supervisory committee members of the Chinese Pharmaceutical Industry Trade Union; Reception: Jiang Wenfang, Huang Saizhong, Sheng Xinru. After the ceremony, Chairman Xie Liheng delivered the opening remarks, saying that the establishment of a memorial day must have a meaning and its mission. On the static side, it is to make everyone not forget this day of historical value. On the dynamic side, it is to encourage everyone to work hard to expand the excitement given by this day, so that new life and new glory can reach the state of creation from excitement. Therefore, the arrival of a memorial day is a wake-up call for reflection, absolutely different from a story dramatized in such a plain way. When the second March 17th memorial arrives, due to reflection, we trace the historical facts of the March 17th memorial: 1. The national medical and pharmaceutical circles rose up and united to seek transformation on March 17th of the 18th year. 2. The Central National Medical Museum was officially established on March 17th of the 20th year. After the two meanings, the March 17th memorial day was produced. The mission of this memorial day is because imperialists invade weak nations, always using culture and economy as the vanguard of political and military aggression. Medicine and pharmacy are the two major tributaries of culture and economy. Where our duties lie, how can we wait with our hands tied? The first March 17th memorial became the date of general mobilization for the Chinese medicine and pharmaceutical circles to rise up together and stand on the front line of national struggle. The importance of the mission and the seriousness of the meaning are unparalleled. The second and third memorials should be exhibitions of battles, explorations of tactics, and replenishment of combat power, which is what was said earlier, to enable new life and new glory to reach the realm of creation through continuous exploration and replenishment.

Other Remarks

After the chairman's report, the representative of the City Party Headquarters, Mao Xiaxuan, delivered a speech, saying that he firmly believes that the enthusiastic celebration of the National Doctors' Day by the city's national medical community is a manifestation of the spirit of the national medical community. National medicine has a long history of thousands of years and has undeniable characteristics, but due to the conservative and mysterious thinking passed down from the past, national medicine has not been able to make full progress. In the future, this kind of concept should be broken, and scientific methods should be used to conduct open research, so that national medicine can make great progress. In the future, not only will it be valued by the general public in the country, but also countries around the world will be able to confirm that Chinese medicine and Taoism really have their unique characteristics that are beyond the reach of the medicine of various countries. Then, the representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, Mao Shenghe, delivered a speech, saying that the reason why national medicine in China has been able to continue for thousands of years without being replaced must have its characteristics. Today, countries around the world have paid attention to Chinese medical theory and are conducting practical research, which shows that Chinese medical theory really has the value of existence. He congratulated everyone on using past experiences and knowledge to strive for the improvement of national medicine, and there will definitely be unlimited hope in the future, and it will also have a great contribution to human health. There were also speeches by Nie Haifan of the City Education Bureau and Tao Leqin of the National Federation of Commerce, and the words were omitted from the length.

Meeting Slogans

The National Postal Workers' General Assembly's Third National Congress Held Its Third and Fourth Meetings Yesterday, Continuing to Discuss Proposals on Bureau Affairs, Treatment, and Benefits. Five Local Groups Held a Joint Banquet in the Evening. - The Opening Ceremony Will Be Held This Afternoon - 107

The Third National Congress of the National Postal Workers' General Union continued its third official meeting at 9:00 AM yesterday, continuing to discuss proposals from the Bureau Affairs Group. At 2:00 PM, the fourth official meeting was held to discuss proposals from the Treatment Group, chaired by Lu Jingshi and Zhang Guangdai respectively. Several important cases were resolved. Details are as follows:

Consolidating Proposals: The number of proposals from each group was very large. Those that were similar had been reviewed and consolidated by the review committees of each group over the past few days. The number of proposals deemed worthy of presentation to the Congress was as follows: 17 from the General Affairs Group, 50 from the Bureau Affairs Group, 21 from the Treatment Group, and 9 from the Welfare Group.

Third Meeting: The third official meeting was held at 9:00 AM yesterday. 58 delegates were present, and 4 observers. After the chairman, Zhang Guangdai, and the recorders, Chen Shihao and Gu Xizhang, performed the formalities, the chairman reported that the proposals from the Bureau Affairs Group had not yet been fully discussed yesterday and that the current meeting would continue the discussion. The Secretary-General then reported that more than a dozen congratulatory telegrams had been received from the postal workers' unions of Bengbu, Xichuan, Fuzhou, and the Jinpu Railway Union.

Improving Bureau Affairs: After the report, the discussion of proposals began. Many proposals to improve bureau affairs were resolved. The more important ones were: The local unions should thoroughly investigate the situation after the merger of postal and telegraph services and report to the General Union for handling. A letter should be sent to the press and publishing circles in various regions, suggesting that the packaging method for printed matter should adopt a flat format to facilitate speed. It was suggested that the postal authorities should add guards to maintain public safety. Improve all sanitary equipment in local bureaus and offices. Regarding the illegal punishment by the authorities of postal workers in Peiping and Tianjin, the General Union has previously negotiated with the commissioners and workers, which has been largely resolved, and the punishments have been canceled. However, there are still several people who have been resented by the authorities because of this case, have had their performance reports downgraded, and have not been transferred to neighboring postal areas. The General Union will actively negotiate with the authorities to restore the original performance reports and transfer them to nearby postal areas.

Temporary Motions: After the above proposals were discussed, two temporary motions were put forward by the attending representatives: Re-telegraph Minister Yu, ordering the return of the over-deducted flood relief donations, which was passed. The Qingdao Postal Workers' Union telegraphed, reporting that the director of the bureau was arrogant and undermined labor movements, and requested that measures be taken to protect them. It was resolved to send a telegram in the name of the Congress to warn the director.

Fourth Meeting: The fourth meeting was convened at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. 59 delegates and 4 observers were present. The meeting was chaired by Lu Jingshi, and the recorders were Chen Shihao and Gu Xizhang. Proposals from the Welfare Group, the General Affairs Group, and the Treatment Group were discussed. There were a total of eight proposals from the Welfare Group. The more important ones were as follows: Request the postal authorities to establish elementary schools for the children of employees, and where elementary schools have been established, add secondary schools. Run postal workers' consumer cooperatives. Ask the authorities to earnestly promote employee sports in accordance with regulations to improve health. Request the postal authorities to run postal workers' credit small loans. Request the postal authorities to allocate funds to subsidize the General Union to establish a postal workers' correspondence school, and urge the authorities to set up employee refresher courses in first-class bureaus and above to improve intelligence and cultivate talents. Establish postal workers' hospitals and request the authorities to allocate funds, etc. Then, the four unfinished proposals from the General Affairs Group were discussed, as well as various proposals from the Treatment Group, such as negotiating the re-establishment of the examination system, improving medical treatment for postal workers, improving the postal worker guarantee system, preferential treatment for Northeast postal workers, etc., for more than ninety cases.

Today's Agenda: The fifteenth meeting will be held at 9:00 AM this morning to continue discussing the Treatment Group's and other cases, and to re-elect the second executive and supervisory committees. The closing ceremony will be held at 2:00 PM this afternoon.

Group Banquet: At 7:00 PM last night, the International Labour Office China Branch, the China General Chamber of Industry, the China Labour Association, the Ningbo Association, and the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, and other five major groups, specially hosted a joint banquet at the Atlantic Western Restaurant for the national representatives, and were warmly welcomed by Cheng Haifeng, Qian Chengxu, Wang Jianmao, Li Mengnan, Shao Yunbai, and Dong Xinqin, etc. During the banquet, Director Cheng Haifeng and Commissioner Zhou Xuexiang delivered welcome speeches, and Zheng Tingjie, a representative of Xichuan, delivered a reply. The hosts and guests enjoyed themselves and dispersed. It is said that the National Postal Workers' General Union will hold a banquet at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA at 7:00 PM tonight.

Wan Hang: Forced Execution of Rent, False Deposits, and Deductions - Instruction from the Ministry of Judicial Administration 108

The Second and Third Branches of the Jiangsu High Court yesterday received Instruction No. 755 from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, which stated that the Judicial Yuan's Instruction No. 75 (訓字) of February 5 of this year approved the Executive Yuan's dispatch of January 25, which stated that due to the impact of the market downturn in cities, the number of cases of landlords suing tenants for rent has been increasing. Even when judgments are confirmed, tenants often abscond, making enforcement impossible. It seems appropriate to consult the Judicial Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Judicial Administration to order all courts and judicial offices to strictly enforce provisional attachment and provisional execution separately in accordance with the provisions of the Code of Civil Procedure to maintain the credibility of the court and the rights of the parties. This matter has been submitted to the 246th resolution meeting of this court, resolved and recorded. Please comply with the above. In addition to responding to the consultation, this document is to instruct the department to investigate and order compliance, and to instruct the subordinate bodies to comply.
