Two Charitable Organizations Jointly Conclude Winter Relief in Shuyang 112

The China International Famine Relief Commission and the Chinese Relief Society have jointly concluded the winter relief effort in Muyang, Jiangsu, and have submitted a report this month. A total of six townships in the seventh district, including Kelang, Lianhualongji, Baodang, Mengdun, and Zhouji, and eight townships in the eighth district, including Machang, Yanbei, Yannan, Fanwan, Xiping, Nanping, Zhongzheng, and Xiaodian, have been provided with assistance. The total number of people assisted was 12,200 adults and 7,531 children, with a total of 1,758 shi and 1 dou of corn distributed. In addition, 3,000 sets of cotton clothing were distributed in the 7th, 8th, and 9th districts and the urban area. Each person received only 9 sheng of corn, and only the poorest received a set of cotton clothing. The relief was minimal compared to the severity of the disaster, and could only save a few people. The winter period has just passed, and the spring famine is coming again. The people in the disaster area are starving and freezing all day long, and cannot avoid filling the gullies. According to the report from the eighth district of the county, the eighth district is located in eastern Shuyang, and the land is low-lying. It used to be one of the water towns. Every time there is a mountain flood, all the fields become swamps. Last autumn, the Yellow River breached its banks, and the flood flowed horizontally, turning the entire area into a sea. Villages and houses were destroyed. Fortunately, the two associations came to provide food and clothing last winter, which allowed the people to survive. At that time, the disaster victims either carried unwashed grain or sought help from relatives and friends, which could barely sustain them. Now that the flood has returned to the channel, there is a desire to return but no way to do so. There is a time for sowing seeds, but there is a shortage of millet. There is a need to complete the gathering, but there is no way to resist hunger. The actual number of households in this situation has reached more than 7,000, which is several times more than the number investigated during the fall. In this spring famine, the people are waiting to be fed. This situation is unbearable. Since food has been provided in the past, it is hoped that relief will come again in the future. We sincerely hope that people will be saved thoroughly, and we dare to present the disaster situation and plead for the people. In this spring famine, when hunger and cold are intertwined, how can people in the world rise up to provide relief and save the remaining lives in the gullies from death?

Certificates Issued by Trade Associations Do Not Need to Be Stamped 113

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce responded yesterday to a letter from the Engineering and Construction Industry Association regarding the matter of whether trade certificates issued by the association need to be stamped, stating, "We have received your letter of the 16th of this month, stating that your association must issue a certificate before members of the industry register with the Bureau of Public Works. You have requested that we investigate whether this certificate should be stamped. Article 1 of the Stamp Tax Law stipulates that all types of certificates stipulated in this law shall pay stamp tax in accordance with this law. In other words, certificates not stipulated in this law are not required to be stamped. This is one of the main points of this law that should be recognized first. Item 28 of Article 16 of the Stamp Tax Law, 'Certificates for proving identity or qualifications,' states under the heading 'Nature' that all types of certificates and licenses issued by the competent authorities to prove the identity or qualifications of the people fall under this category. Therefore, the stamping of certificates under this item is limited to those issued by the competent authorities. Certificates not issued by the government are not within the scope of this item and are not required to be stamped according to law."

Masterpieces of Painting from Jin, Tang, Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing Dynasties Published - Compiled by Liu Haisu 120

This book is published by the China Book Company and compiled by Mr. Liu Haisu through long-term collection and compilation. The entire book is in four volumes. The first volume is a general theory of Chinese painting of 100,000 words, which describes in detail the origin and evolution of painting schools throughout the ages, as well as the living conditions, thoughts, and trends of painters. The front of the volume has seven color plates: Arhat, made by Guanxiu in the Five Dynasties; Hollyhock, made by Li Di in the Song Dynasty; Arhat, made by Li Lin in the Song Dynasty; Daylily and Puppies, made by Mao Yi in the Song Dynasty; Caressing Solitary Pine and Wandering, made by Zhao Mengfu in the Yuan Dynasty; Pheasant, made by Wang Yuan in the Yuan Dynasty; and Jingu Map, made by Qiu Ying in the Ming Dynasty. The second volume contains paintings from the Jin, Tang, Five Dynasties, and Song Dynasties, with carefully selected works by Gu Kaizhi, Yan Liben, Li Zhaodao, Wu Daozi, Wang Wei, Bian Luan, Zhou Fang, Dai Song, Xu Xi, Zhou Wenju, Li Sheng, Du Xiao, Li Cheng, Xu Daoning, Fan Kuan, Guo Zhongshu, Zhao Chang, Guo Xi, Yan Wengui, Zhao Lingrang, Su Shi, Mi Fu, Li Di, Mi Youren, Li Tang, Liang Kai, Liu Songnian, Ma Lin, Ma Yuan, Ma Xingzu, Diao Guangyin, Xia Gui, Yan Jueping, Ma Kui, Gong Kai, Muxi, Song Di, and Xu Chongsi, a total of 57 paintings. The third volume contains paintings from the Yuan and Ming Dynasties, with carefully selected works by Zhao Mengfu, Guan Daosheng, Zhao Yong, Wang Yuan, Yan Hui, Huang Gongwang, Wang Meng, Ni Zan, Wu Zhen, Sheng Mao, Xia Mingyuan, Dai Jin, Wu Wei, Shen Zhou, Lin Liang, Lv Ji, Zhou Chen, Tang Yin, Qiu Ying, Wen Zhengming, Chen Daofu, Xu Lin, Zhu Duan, Xia Wenyu, Sheng Maohua, Zhang Hong, Huang Qichang, Xie Shichen, Li Liufang, Zhang Ruoyuan, Ni Yuanlang, Wang Jianzhang, Wang Duo, Shi Rui, Lan Ying, Wang E, Ji Ru, Yun Xiang, Qi Zhijia, Wang Siren, Yang Wencong, and Zhang Xuezeng, a total of 80 paintings. The fourth volume contains paintings from the Qing Dynasty, with carefully selected works by Wang Shimin, Wang Jian, Wang Hui, Wang Yuanqi, Wu Li, Yun Ge, Shi Xi, Bada Shanren, Shi Tao, Fang Dayou, Yuan Xue, Sun Kehong, Gong Xian, Gao Cen, Shen Quan, Shen Zongjing, Zou Zhe, Lang Shining, Sun Fu, Li Shizuo, Hua Yan, Huang Shen, Jin Nong, Luo Ping, Shi Hongren, Gu Dashen, Mei Qing, Luo Mu, Gao Qipei, Cha Shibiao, Huang Ji, Xu You, Tang Mi, Li Shizhuo, Bian Shoumin, Jiang Tingxi, Dong Bangda, Wang Zhen, Zhang Zongcang, Shen Zongqian, Zhang Geng, Xi Gang, Dai Xi, Gai Qi, Ma Xiangjiang, Zhao Zhiqian, Ren Xun, and other representative works of 85 frames. Each volume is sold for only 2.5 yuan and is printed on copperplate paper. If there are any blurry or unclear prints, they will be selected and reprinted. The selected paintings are all representative works of the great masters of each era and have never been printed in the market before. This huge work is truly spectacular. It is not only for the study of artists and scholars, but also a treasure for the international art community. Since its publication, the Shanghai China Book Company has sold more than 1,000 copies. Scholars from the East and the West have said that this is an unprecedented masterpiece for the systematic study and verification of Chinese painting.

The Bureau of Public Works Announces the Registration List of Physicians, Dentists, and Veterinarians 121

The Shanghai Public Concession Bureau of Public Works' 1936 registration list of physicians, dentists, and veterinarians is now scheduled to be announced tomorrow (Thursday) as one of the Bureau of Public Works' public reports. The list currently contains 1,005 practicing physicians, 167 dentists, and 19 veterinarians. Among them, there are 100 Chinese medicine practitioners registered with the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau. Analyzing by nationality, among the practicing physicians, there are 676 Chinese, 64 Japanese, 55 Russian, and 56 American. There are 10 Japanese and 5 British. The importance of this list lies in the fact that all physicians, dentists, and veterinarians listed in this book have been officially registered. Those who are not named in this book have not completed the registration procedure. Furthermore, the Shanghai Medical Board was established on April 1, 1931. All physicians, dentists, and veterinarians who apply for registration must pass the examination of the board and its review subcommittee. Last year, 118 physicians who applied for registration in Shanghai were approved, 13 dentists were registered, and 2 veterinarians were registered. 21 registrations were revoked, including 3 deaths, 14 departures from Shanghai, 3 suspensions of practice, and 1 removal from the list.

In the future, the number of lottery numbers will gradually increase to 50,000 yuan if it exceeds 50,000 numbers. Now that the association is just starting, there are not many numbers included in the lottery, so it is easy to win. In addition, the association's regulations have various preferential features for savers that are different from previous savings associations, so savers are vying to join.

China Industrial Gas Company - Successful Experiment in Self-Made Calcium Carbide 123

The China Industrial Gas Company, located at 537 Liaoyang Road, has been established for many years, producing industrial raw materials such as oxygen, carbon dioxide, and light gas, which have long been sold throughout the country and have earned a good reputation. Later, due to calcium carbide being a necessity for the welding industry and a major raw material for manufacturing carbon dioxide and other industrial products such as acetic acid, alcohol, fertilizer, glue, graphite, etc., it was previously imported in large quantities. Since there were no domestically produced goods, the company was always subject to foreign control. Therefore, several years ago, the company planned to produce its own, and after arduous efforts, it was finally produced in February of this year. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited the factory and saw the calcium carbide produced. According to Guo Chengen, the chairman of the company, the electricity consumption is no less than four or five times cheaper per unit than using hydroelectric power from foreign countries. The production costs are being reduced. However, the original motivation for self-manufacturing was to stop the leakages and strive for self-reliance, and all the raw materials used are domestic products. Therefore, the company does not hesitate to make significant sacrifices to conduct an industrial experiment, and it will continue to research and gradually improve in the hope that this industrial raw material can be self-sufficient.

Purpose

The hall is located on the third floor of the Jianghai Customs House. Polish Traveling Journalist Couple Arrives in Shanghai on a Far East Tour - Will Stay in China for a Year for Sightseeing and Investigation - Total Journey Reaches More Than 20,000 Miles 126

In the autumn of 1934, they departed from Warsaw, the capital of Poland, via Berlin, Bourg Land, Vienna, Safia, Constantinople, Cola, Arapu, Badastan, Dehelen, Guopei, Delhi Sea, Bombay, Benares, Calcutta, and Rangoon, and then entered China via Longzhou, a border town in Guangxi, through Hanoi and Dong Dang in Annam. Then they followed the Guangxi Highway to Nanning, Wuzhou, and then to Guangzhou before transferring to Shantou and coming to Shanghai. They arrived in Shanghai on the 16th and stayed at the Polish Overseas Chinese Association. Yesterday, a reporter visited them. The Polish couple was covered in dust, and the motorized bicycle they were riding was covered in yellow mud, which was a testament to their hard work on the journey. According to them, this journey relied entirely on this motorized bicycle as a means of transportation. Since departing from Warsaw on August 23, 1934, to the day they arrived in Shanghai, they have traveled 34,300 kilometers, crossing the Great Desert and various tropical regions. Although the journey was extremely difficult, they were able to personally experience various countries and investigate their social customs, which was infinitely interesting. Before departure, they received introductions from the embassy in your country, and after entering your country, they received various conveniences from the authorities of various provinces, for which we are deeply grateful. The scenery of your country is beautiful, and the cultural relics are rich, which makes people have infinite admiration. They planned to rest in Shanghai for a while, and then take the original bicycle to visit various ports in your country, expecting to stay in China for a year before returning home. When we stayed in Nanning, we were specially entertained by Huang Xuchu, the chairman of the Guangxi Provincial Government, and toured various places. The trip from Longzhou to Shanghai, including the stopovers along the way, took a total of twenty-three days. We are correspondents for the Warsaw newspaper in Poland, and we will attach photos of what we have seen along the way and send them back to our country for publication. When asked about the situation of Polish newspapers, they said that Polish newspapers are now very developed. There are fifteen famous daily newspapers in Warsaw, and the largest circulation is 250,000 copies per day. The newspaper we represent has two daily newspapers, two evening newspapers, and four weekly newspapers, for a total of seven. They also said that after we came to your country, we ate your country's meals every day, which have a unique flavor and are inexhaustible. It is truly the most famous food in the world. The motorcycle we ride is a Three Guns brand motorcycle, which is sturdy and durable. It has traveled tens of thousands of miles and is still intact. What is even more amazing is that the Dunlop tires we used when we set off from Poland have not been changed, which can also be introduced.

Dredging Bureau Adds New Gigantic Mud Dredging Wheel - The Divine Shoal Has Been Dredged for Two Miles - Bidding Invited for the Construction of Gigantic Wheel 127

In order to dredge the Divine Shoal at the mouth of the Yangtze River outside the Wusong Estuary, the Shanghai Dredging Bureau ordered a giant mud dredging wheel called the Jianshe from Germany last year. It is currently working at the Divine Shoal. At the same time, the bureau continues to order another similar mud dredging wheel. The hull of the ship is larger than the Jianshe and the mud suction power is also increased. The bureau will start inviting merchants with extensive experience from all countries to bid for the construction today. The Datong News Agency reporter has recorded the situation as follows.

Completion of Divine Shoal

According to Dr. Chadley, the chief engineer of the bureau, the Divine Shoal has recently been completed. The dredging work on the shoal has reached two miles, and the amount of mud removed is estimated to be 500,000 cubic meters (4 tons per cubic meter). Work is still limited to daytime, and in the future, plans will be made to add nighttime work. The progress of the completion of the dredging is extremely smooth.

Addition of New Machine

The bureau plans to add a mud dredging wheel of the same size as the Jianshe. It is now possible to start inviting shipyards with extensive experience from all countries to construct the wheel. The hull of this mud dredging wheel should be slightly larger than the Jianshe. It is a seagoing suction dredger, which can operate normally without anchoring when it has a mud hold. It is the world's most advanced mud dredging wheel, personally designed by Chadley. Regarding the dredging efficiency, it only needs to work ten hours a day to dredge 20,000 cubic yards of solidified sand and mud in the Yangtze River and can continue to drive to a mud disposal site two miles away. After the bidding for the mud dredging wheel starts today, if European shipyards submit bidding letters, they must be sent from Siberia to expedite delivery and avoid delays. It is also learned that the magnitude and mud dredging efficiency of the wood-hulled mud dredging wheel will match any mud dredging wheel in the world.

Cancellation of Contract for Receiving Banknotes Still in Dispute - Twenty-Five Qian Zhuang File Suit - Continental Bank and President Ye Fuxiao Accused - Requesting Confirmation That Cancellation of Contract is Invalid and Compensation for Profits 128

Since the Ministry of Finance reformed the currency system last winter, banks that had contracts with Qian Zhuang (traditional Chinese banks) to sell secretly marked banknotes (i.e., banknotes) generally wanted to take the opportunity to cancel the contracts, which led to lawsuits. For example, the Continental and Donglai banks had been sued for breach of contract by Qian Zhuang that were receiving the banknotes. The two banks then brought in people to mediate and resolve the disputes. However, before the Continental Bank was sued by Hua Feng and thirteen other Qian Zhuang, it had already canceled the contract for receiving banknotes with Bao Kang and twenty-five other Qian Zhuang. At that time, the Continental Bank told the Qian Zhuang receiving the banknotes that the contract signed under the instructions of the Ministry was no longer applicable to Bao Kang and other Qian Zhuang, who mistakenly believed that it was sincere. As a result, they accepted the unconditional cancellation of the contract. Later, after learning that the Continental Bank had been sued by Hua Feng and other Qian Zhuang, they learned that those with banknotes had settled the case, and they knew that the Continental Bank had done this. They felt that Ye Fuxiao, the president of the bank, should not have treated them differently, causing them unnecessary losses. Therefore, Bao Kang, Qing Kang, Yucheng, Hengmao, Hongfu, Yucheng, Lianyi, Hongkang, Hongchang, Hongda, Dingyuan, Lianxing, Yuanheng, Shuntai, Yongtai, Yucheng, Yongtai, Zhenxing, Tonghe, Hongmao, Qiantai, Shuntai, Yufeng, and Fukang, twenty-five Qian Zhuang jointly hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to sue the Continental Bank and its president, Ye Fuxiao, in the District Court of the First Special District. The plaintiffs stated that they had contracted to receive a total of 3.05 million yuan in banknotes, and the contract stipulated the important rights and obligations of both parties. The obligations of the plaintiffs were to promote the banknotes in accordance with the contract and deposit the reserve funds for the returned amount with the defendant. The obligations of the defendant were to pay interest at 40% of the reserve funds in accordance with the contract. Both parties fulfilled the contract without any problems. Unexpectedly, on November 4 of last year, they suddenly received a letter from the defendant stating that, due to the unified issuance and centralized preparation, the contract for receiving banknotes was no longer applicable and should be canceled immediately. After receiving the letter, the plaintiffs repeatedly consulted with the defendant to maintain the original contract, but the defendant refused, saying that the Ministry's instructions were no longer applicable, and who would dare to violate them? They also said that if they did not hand over the contract, they would not be paid the interest they were entitled to. The plaintiffs had inquired about the experiences of others who had contacted the defendant, and the answers were consistent. They believed that operating a bank required a strong sense of trust and that the defendant would not intentionally deceive them. Therefore, they reluctantly handed over the contracts that had not yet expired. However, the intention and behavior of handing over the contracts were not voluntary. The means by which the defendant carried out the contract can be said to be obvious. Although the plaintiffs were deceived for a while, they were not willing to accept it. Therefore, they investigated the truth of the Ministry's order and found that the plaintiffs had been fooled by the defendant. The order issued by the Ministry of Finance was only a few months old, and the Central China banknotes were still circulating in the market, which was clear evidence. Moreover, the Central Bank has now established regulations for receiving banknotes, which are no different from the regulations for receiving banknotes signed by the original parties. The defendant's letter falsely stated that the Ministry of Finance's order was not applicable to the regulations for receiving banknotes, which was fraudulent. The fact that the defendant was sued by the Zha Chang Zhuang and others in the High Court in the same case and knew that it was in the wrong, and that it had desperately begged people to reconcile with the plaintiff in the case and pay interest to settle the case, further proved that the defendant's cancellation

The original plaintiff's contract

Was an act of using fraud to exercise its rights under the law, and the act of fraudulently eliminating the rights of others should be confirmed as invalid. According to Article 92 of the Civil Code, if a declaration of intent is made due to fraud or coercion, the declarant may revoke his declaration of intent. Article 101, paragraph 2, states that if a party who benefits from the fulfillment of a condition improperly promotes the fulfillment of the condition, the condition shall be deemed not to have been fulfilled. Moreover, the previous judgment of the High Court stated that "fraud" in civil law refers to intentionally showing untruthful matters to the other party, causing them to fall into error and make a declaration of intent due to the error. Another previous judgment stated that if the establishment of a legal act

Due to fraud or coercion

To the extent that the declaration of intent made by the parties is not free, in order to protect the declarer, they should be allowed to revoke it. It is found that since the plaintiffs in this case signed the contract with the defendant, the obligations they have fulfilled have been considerable. Therefore, the existence of this contract has considerable rights to be recovered. If the defendant had not intentionally used fraud and threatened with the Ministry's order, the plaintiff would have been willing to abandon its rights and make a declaration of cancellation. The handing over of the contract by the plaintiffs was clearly not of their own free will, and the fulfillment of the condition of unconditional cancellation was purely promoted by the defendant's improper behavior. The condition of cancellation should be deemed not to have been fulfilled. Based on the above reasons, in accordance with the above-mentioned legal precedents, it is requested that the defendant be summoned to court to render a judgment confirming that the defendant's act of canceling the contract is

The act is invalid

And compensate the plaintiffs for the benefits they should have enjoyed under each contract and bear the litigation costs. The defendant then hired lawyers such as Wang Zhuan to file a statement of defense. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Mo Runhua of the First Special Court opened a court hearing. Zhan Jifeng, the plaintiff's attorney, first stated the intent of the lawsuit, saying that the guarantee money paid by the plaintiff in accordance with the contract was set at 40% in cash. Since the reform of the currency system, the defendant believed that the 40% in cash was also legal tender, and that from then on, banknotes would be exchanged for banknotes, and they did not want to pay the agreed interest. Therefore, they sent a letter to each plaintiff saying that they were acting on the order of the Ministry and had to cancel the contract, otherwise the interest before November 3 would not be paid. At that time, each plaintiff

Because the Ministry's order was difficult to disobey, each handed over the contract. However, other banknote recipients with better knowledge or thought, fearing that they would be deceived, sued the bank. As a result, the bank saw that it could not use threats and reconciled with them, paying all the interest. Later, the plaintiff learned that the Ministry of Finance had not issued any orders, so they negotiated with the defendant again. The defendant suddenly changed its tone and no longer said that it was acting on the order of the Ministry but said that it was due to the Ministry's order. This shows that the defendant was actually using a kind of tactic at that time to cancel the contract. Therefore, it is requested that the act of canceling the contract be confirmed as invalid, and that the defendant be ordered to pay the original interest of 85,667 yuan, 6 jiao, and 6 fen. The defendant's lawyer replied, first saying that the contract for receiving banknotes was based on the bank's right to issue banknotes,

Today's issuance is stopped

Since there is no need to promote sales, he went on to say that the plaintiff's cancellation of the contract was not accompanied by threats, fraud, or improper means. Finally, he said that the case of Fuchang and others suing the Continental Bank did not result in a reconciliation between the Continental Bank and the plaintiffs of the case automatically withdrew the lawsuit. The plaintiff's lawyer then refuted them one by one, saying that receiving banknotes and issuing banknotes were two completely different things. The defendant deliberately distorted the truth, and other banks that were no longer issuing banknotes were still continuing to fulfill the contract for receiving banknotes, and Donglai even signed a new one. As for the lawsuit filed by Fuchang and others, if the defendant had not paid interest to settle the case, how could it have been willing to withdraw halfway? In short, the defendant threatens those who are weak and reconciles with those who cannot be deceived. After both sides had finished arguing, Judge Mo decided to announce the judgment at noon on the 23rd of this month.

Taisun's Dangerous Crossing - Horrific Waves and Yellow Sand

The China Merchants Bureau's Taisun, which was returning to Shanghai from Shantou this time, was supposed to carry 5,000 bags of domestic sugar to Shanghai as usual. Unexpectedly, the bureau telegraphed the ship to go to Xiamen as well. Sugar merchants in Shantou stopped loading because the ship's detour to Xiamen would take more days. As a result, the Taisun sailed to Xiamen empty, thinking it could load cargo to ballast the ship. Unexpectedly, it only carried dozens of steerage passengers to Xiamen. The ship's hull rose and fell suddenly, and the captain Jiang Changqing went through all kinds of hardships before avoiding an accident. However, the outer side of the iron plate had already been smashed with a hole by the storm showing the fierceness of the waves. Fortunately, it was filled in time and was able to continue sailing. When it reached the waters off Wenzhou, it encountered yellow sand covering the sea, making it impossible to see anything in front of it, similar to a heavy fog. Fortunately, Captain Jiang was familiar with the waterway and was not in danger. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday and was still trembling with fear when he spoke. The damaged hole in the hull has been reported to the head office for immediate repair.

Yang Xien, a local man, was nearly thirty years old and lived at No. 24 Zhujia Shed, Haige Road. During the day, he worked at the Shanghai Hospital on Haige Road. Therefore, when Yang walked into the house, he was surprised to find that it was silent. In a panic, the bandits caught a glimpse of Yang Xien and thought that the matter had been leaked and detectives had arrived. They panicked and pulled out their pistols, firing three shots in a row, knocking Yang down. Tang Lingxun, the daughter of the landlord Tang, was also shot. The bandits then left the house and fled. When the bandits had gone far away, his family members ran out to see what had happened. They saw that Yang had been shot in the abdomen and Tang Lingxun had been shot in the leg. Counterfeit Subsidiary Coins Discovered Two Criminals Detained Awaiting Sentencing 136

Feng Baishun, a detective from the Chengdu Road Police Station, contacted Li Zongzhang, a Jiangbei native representing Liu Zhi, who stated that 35 counterfeit nickel coins could be purchased for one yuan. Detective Ma went to Liu's house, but Liu had already fled. Liu's concubine, Liu Li, was arrested, and five counterfeit five-cent lead coins, a five-cent plaster model, ten taels of lead, and miscellaneous items such as plaster powder and seals were confiscated and taken back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. When questioned, Liu Li confessed that she had been living with Liu Wenrong for only five months and that Liu had been secretly manufacturing these lead coins at night in collaboration with Li Zongzhang and Wu Dakezi for the past five days, and that she had not helped. Judge Wu Zehan reviewed the confessions and ordered that the two defendants be returned to custody to await sentencing on the 21st.

Cai Wenxin (also known as Wenming) from Tongzhou lost his wife early and left behind a daughter, Yueying, who is now eight years old. Cai recently married Hu, a woman from Suzhou, as his second wife. They live together at No. 16, Lane 583, Zhejiang Road. Hu is extremely fierce and abuses Yueying in every way, beating her severely several times, causing the girl to be covered in scars and bruises. Kong Zaoxian and Qiu A'quan, who live in the same house, could not bear to watch and reported it to the Laozha Police Station, who sent Detective Qiu Sijiu to arrest Cai Wenxin and Cai Hu. This information has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, Judge Qian Hongye continued the hearing in the First Criminal Court. The police station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, requested that the court release the forensic report for review. According to the forensic report, Cai Yueying's head, face, chest, abdomen, back, shoulders, and buttocks all had injuries, and her wrists and neck had rope marks. The court then ordered Cai Yueying to be brought to the court to inquire about the source of the rope marks. She confessed that her mother tied her hands and neck with a rope because she was slow in doing things. The two defendants continued to deny everything. The court then summoned Cai Wenxin's brother, Wenbiao, to the court and asked if he could take Cai Yueying back to be cared for and educated instead of leaving her with Cai Wenxin. He replied that he could do so. After mutual arguments between the two lawyers, Judge Qian announced the verdict: Cai Hu was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for abusing a young girl and hindering her physical development. Cai Wenxin was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the same crime, suspended for two years. During the probation period, he will be supervised by the police station. Cai Wenbiao was ordered to provide bail and submit a written request to the court to take Cai Yueying.

Little Putuo Bridge Widow Dies Suddenly, Coffin Opened for Autopsy 141

Feng Zhang, a widow aged 40 from Nanhui, residing at No. 94, Little Putuo Bridge in Nanshi, suddenly died suddenly on the seventh night of this year's lunar calendar. The local headman reported it to the local court, which sent someone to determine that Feng Zhang had died from poisoning, as reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that she was adopted as a child bride but unexpectedly, before she was formally married, her fiancé died of illness. She considered herself unlucky, practiced vegetarianism and worshipped Buddha, and endured hardship to maintain her chastity for over twenty years. Relatives and neighbors praised her. She usually spent her days chanting scriptures with Feng Songtao, an elderly man in his seventies. (Feng Songtao used to be a clerk at Jiu Ji Bei Zhan in Nanshi, but now he is too old to perform his duties, so his eldest son, Feng Zilin, has taken his place.) However, after the incident, Feng Zilin, the husband's elder brother of the deceased, noticed that the items in the room were in a mess, and the clothes in the box were all gone. Neighbors also testified that on the evening of the incident, at around 8:00 PM, Zhu A'er, a tailor who was the deceased's nephew, and a young man came to visit his aunt (the deceased). After the tragedy was discovered the next day, Zhu A'er and others disappeared without a trace. It is possible that Feng Zhang was designed to be poisoned by Zhu A'er and others. Therefore, he filed a complaint with the court requesting justice. Yesterday, Prosecutor Li Xulin ordered Feng Zilin to be summoned to court for questioning. Although it had been determined that Feng Zhang had died from poisoning, what kind of poison was still unknown. To clarify the truth, Feng Zilin was ordered to send Feng Zhang's coffin to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for an autopsy immediately. At the same time, Zhu A'er and others were ordered to be arrested for further investigation.

Zhang Cailan, a local man who is a Taoist priest and resides in Chenjiazhai, across from Guanghua University on Daxilu, West Shanghai, was playing mahjong with Lu Jigen and others, villagers from Lujiazhai, Fahuaxi Town, in Yao A'mao's teahouse in Chen Geng Lane the day before yesterday afternoon. Central Bank Inspection Report 143

The 274th Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of Central Bank Exchange Vouchers states: In accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the number of exchange vouchers issued by this bank and the reserve fund. The 274th inspection was conducted on March 14, 25th year of the Republic of China, at the issuing bureau of this bank. The inspection results are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange vouchers issued is 24,117,8254 silver dollars, including 21,804,0484 silver dollars and 2,3137,770 subsidiary currency vouchers. The total amount of exchange voucher reserve fund is 24,117,8254 yuan, including a cash reserve of 16,341,4374 yuan. The cash reserve is kept in the issuing branches and sub-branches of this bank (13,179,2846.71 yuan), in other banks (3,162,1527.29 yuan), and a guarantee reserve of 7,776,3880 yuan converted into silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange vouchers issued is 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of the customs gold exchange voucher reserve fund is 373,324.70 yuan. The reserve fund includes 7,351 taels and 9 qian and 5 fen of gold, which is converted to 373,324.70 yuan based on the fixed price of 50779 yuan for gold. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve must be at least 60%, and the remainder must be a guarantee reserve with legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is hereby made. March 16, 25th year of the Republic of China. Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jiyan.

Letter from Lao Jiu He to Fellow Trade Associations 146

Letter from Lao Jiu He to the Silk and Satin Trade Association regarding the sale of one foot for one cent: Esteemed Sirs, Having read in the newspapers of this month, the 12th, that your esteemed association believes that commercial ethics have been completely destroyed by fellow traders who do not abide by good faith, you have written to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to issue a call for guidance, and to jointly raise commercial ethics in order to save industry and commerce. This bureau sincerely expresses its sympathy. However, this bureau's business has always been based on the principle of long-term, low-price, and high-volume sales. Any special sacrifices are based on facts and truth. Therefore, the unethical behaviors mentioned in your letter, such as selling inferior goods, seeking exorbitant profits, and making false propaganda to deceive customers, are abhorrent to this bureau and have nothing to do with us. There is no need to argue. However, the phrase "even selling silk and satin for one cent to a few cents per foot" is a concern. Upon investigation, no fellow trader has made such a statement recently, except for this bureau. Considering the facts, your association's words are clearly directed at this bureau. However, although there is no such thing as buying one foot for one cent as a common practice in the market, this bureau has the fact of selling one foot for one cent, with accounting books and customers to inquire. (Omitted). In order to support your association's efforts to raise commercial ethics and eliminate false propaganda with facts, this bureau has decided to publicly sell 100 bolts of real silk spun silk for one cent per foot, limited to one zhang per person, from 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM on the 19th of this month, in order to prove that this bureau's previous sale of one foot for one cent was not false, and to give those who claim to have far-sighted vision an even higher and farther understanding. Fearing that doubts will not be resolved and that right and wrong will not be distinguished, we have specially sent this letter to your esteemed association's chairman and request that you forward it to the chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, inviting them to jointly come to the venue for supervision before 9:00 AM on the morning of that day in order to make a great declaration of faith. I believe that your esteemed association will treat all members equally and will not be biased or refuse this request. Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association.

March 17th

Esteemed Chief Editor of the Shen Bao:

I am writing to express my shock and dismay regarding the article published in your paper on the 16th of this month, entitled "Fuan Amusement Park Broadly Advertises: 'Death is Not Compensated,' and Huang Shigong Foolishly Takes the Fall, Bleeding After Being Struck." From my youth to adulthood, I have practiced Chinese martial arts and mastered internal energy cultivation techniques. I previously performed voluntary stage acts at the World Amusement Center disaster relief fundraising event, earning the undeserved title of "Strongman" from the event organizers, a title I find deeply humbling. This time, the Fuan Amusement Park hired the Xiaying Martial Arts Troupe to perform martial arts. Being a friend of the park's director, Wang Rui, I offered to help. Unexpectedly, the Fuan Amusement Park placed large advertisements in various newspapers, changing my name to Wang Zhiqing and inviting the audience to strike my entire body with iron weapons. I was not injured in any way, nor did I bleed. The report in your paper is far from the truth. Upon investigating the advertisements placed by the park, I found them to be outrageous. No one in the world is truly invincible. No expert in Chinese martial arts would dare to make such a boastful and deceptive statement. The park's act of substituting names is unacceptable. If I were to be beaten to death, would I not be giving my life away for nothing? Neither I nor the martial arts troupe have signed any life-or-death contracts with the park. The park's purpose in placing this advertisement is solely to attract an audience and generate revenue at the expense of others' lives. The night before last, I invited my brothers and others to question the park's manager and request to see the life-or-death contract, but we found nothing. This led to a dispute, and we went to the police station together. After the patrol officer clarified the facts, we were released as there was no wrongdoing on our part. There was no matter of a settlement or Bao Qinxuan, the manager of Fuan, posting bail for our release. This matter concerns my lifelong reputation, so I am writing to request a correction, urging your esteemed newspaper to publish it to clarify the facts and correct public perception. I am deeply grateful. Respectfully, I wish you well in your writing endeavors.

Respectfully,

Huang Shigong

March 17th

The Shanghai Fish and Seafood Industry (A Survey of Shanghai's Industry and Commerce, No. 18) 154

I. The Position of the Fish and Seafood Industry in Shanghai. The Qiafeng Faji Fish Shop (Note) and Hengyuan Shenji Fish Shop both closed down last spring.

According to general estimates, Shanghai's annual fish and seafood trade (part of which is salted fish and seafood) exceeded 60 million yuan during its peak. In recent years, with the decline of the market, it still amounts to a huge sum of 15 to 16 million yuan. The importance of Shanghai's fish market is evident from this. The reasons for this can be attributed to two factors: first, Shanghai has a population of over 3.4 million, creating a huge demand; second, it is located on the coast near the river estuary, serving as a hub for the distribution of fish and seafood. Cultured fish from counties like Wuxing, Kunshan, and Wujiang, river fish from various counties along the river, fresh chilled fish and dried salted fish from coastal areas in Zhejiang (such as Yin County, Dinghai County, etc.) and coastal areas in Shandong (such as Qingdao, Weihaiwei, etc.) all rely on Shanghai as their final distribution point. Furthermore, the fish and seafood caught by local fishing vessels are sold entirely in the local market. Therefore, it is no accident that Shanghai has become the only major fish market in the country.

II. Shanghai's Fish Shops and Fishing Vessels

Companies. Shanghai, as a hub for the distribution of fish and seafood, has specialized merchants who act as agents for buying and selling, taking a commission. Due to historical and geographical reasons, these businesses are concentrated in the Xiaodongmen area of the 16th Wharf, including over ten ice-fresh fish shops, five or six freshwater fish shops, and some that operate both. In addition, there are over thirty salted fish shops and over fifty seafood shops (including those that operate both). The ice-fresh fish shops have the highest annual turnover, followed by the freshwater fish shops.

In recent years, the social and economic situation has been poor, and all industries have been affected, including the fish shops, which are no exception. Last year, the Qiafeng Faji Fish Shop (Note 1) and Hengyuan Shenji Fish Shop closed down last spring. The Gongda Fish Shop (Note 2) and Yuantong Xingji Fish Shop also announced liquidation in July of the same year. All of this proves the difficulties of running an ice-fresh fish business. However, overall, the industry is still able to maintain a reasonable profit.

Note 1: After Qiafeng Faji closed down in the spring, they worked hard to resume operations, which was realized in December of the same year. The original partnership was changed to a limited company, renamed Hengji, with a capital of 30,000 yuan divided into 300 shares of 100 yuan each. One-third of the capital was collected, and Zhang Shungen (formerly Lu Jintang) was appointed as manager, and Zhang Xiaochu as supervisor.

Note 2: Gongda also resumed operations in the same month, renamed Gongda Zhongji, with a capital of 18,000 yuan divided into 12 shares. The shareholders were Jiang Ashun, Zhou Yongzhao, and Shi Arong, etc., and Shi Arong was appointed as manager.

As for the salted fish shops in the Xiaodongmen area of the 16th Wharf, although their turnover decreased by 20-30% compared to previous years, they all made a profit due to prudent operations and avoiding bad debts. This is also noted below for reference.

In addition to the fish shops selling fish and seafood, there are also fishing vessel companies engaged in fishing. Shanghai's fishing vessel industry has a history of over thirty years, including both hand-operated net fishing vessels and trawlers. Their current status is listed below:

Note: From Xinghua to Haili, eight are trawlers, and from Chunxing onwards, seven are hand-operated net fishing vessels. Of the aforementioned fifteen companies, except for Jiying, which is a training vessel solely funded by the Xiamen Jimei Fisheries School, the rest are joint-stock companies. Xinghua was reorganized from the former Zhonghua Fisheries Company.

From the above table, we can derive two concepts: first, Shanghai's existing fishing vessel industry is all newly established in recent years; second, the capital and tonnage of the fishing vessels are extremely small. This shows that the economic conditions are a factor contributing to Japanese fishing vessels being able to intrude and fish in China's coastal waters, in addition to general political relations. This is something we should not ignore.

(End)

Jingwu Athletic Association Initiates the Shanghai 30,000-Meter Long-Distance Relay Race 158

In order to actively promote sports, the Jingwu Athletic Association has initiated a 30,000-meter long-distance relay race and welcomes all Shanghai teams to participate. The date is April 12th. The regulations are as follows:

The race will be held at 10:00 AM on April 12th.

Any amateur sports team can register one or more teams to participate in the race.

The competition is team-based. Each team can register six players, but only four players can actually participate.

The race will start from Hongkou Park. The team members will be transported by car to the starting points of their respective sections. After the runners of the first, second, and third sections reach the finish line, they will be picked up by the organizing committee.

The champion team will receive a large silver cup. The second, third, and fourth place teams will each receive a silver cup. Each member of the champion team will receive a silver shield.

Registration is open from now until March 31st at the Jingwu Athletic Association at Yokohamabashi or the Jingwu Public Association at Damalu Continental Emporium. The registration fee is two yuan per team (this registration fee will be refunded after the team officially participates).

Predicting the World Cup Football Champion in the Midst of Turmoil 163

The Netherlands Has Strong Strength and Ambitious Aspirations to Win the Championship

Assuming that the 10th World Games, to be held in Berlin this August, is not affected by the abolition of Germany, the Netherlands has a good chance of winning the football championship. Uruguay is the current Olympic football champion, having won the final against Argentina in 1928 in the Dutch capital. There was no football program at the 10th World Games held in Los Angeles, USA in 1932. The Dutch football team is very strong and has a record of ten victories against European countries, although they have not played against South American teams. In 1931, they defeated Denmark in Copenhagen 2-0. In 1931, they defeated France in Paris 4-3. In 1932, they defeated Belgium in Brussels 3-2. In 1932, they defeated Germany in Dusseldorf 2-0. In 1933, they defeated Belgium in Antwerp 3-1. In 1934, they defeated Belgium in Antwerp 4-2. In 1934, they defeated Switzerland in Bern 4-2. In 1935, they defeated Belgium in Brussels 2-0. In 1935, they defeated Ireland in Dublin 5-3. In 1936, they defeated France in Paris 6-0. The Dutch football team is composed of diverse members, but they all participate as amateurs. They include a police officer, a hotel waiter, a milkman, a chauffeur, two junior clerks, and two students. They only have the opportunity to practice in their spare time. Although they lost to England last year, the defeat was glorious. England played with ten professional players and one amateur player and only narrowly won 2-1. The Dutch team's trainer is the Englishman Glenn Denning. Their tactics have become Anglicized, as has their orange velvet jersey. Their attacking style is to make good use of the wings, and they are also very skilled at heading the ball.

Ministry of Education Orders Delay of Elementary School Spring Break 165

Changed to Start on April 5th

The Previous Day is Children's Day

(Nanjing, 17th) The Ministry of Education, in response to the request from the National Children's Year Implementation Committee to postpone the date of spring break, issued a circular to all departments, stating that since April 4th of this year is Children's Day of Children's Year, in order to facilitate preparations for a large-scale celebration, the spring break for elementary schools this year will be postponed to start on April 5th. All departments are instructed to comply and inform all elementary schools under their jurisdiction to comply accordingly.

One-Year Elementary School Graduates Will Be Given Certificates of Completion 166

(Nanjing, 17th) The Ministry of Education, based on the request from the Zhejiang Department of Education to clarify whether to issue certificates of completion to students who have completed a one-year short-term elementary school course, issued a circular to all departments, stating that students who have completed a one-year short-term elementary school course and passed the examination should be given a certificate of completion by the school. The format of the certificate should be similar to the fourth type of certificate in the regulations for school graduation certificates, with the words "Graduation Certificate" replaced with "Certificate of Completion". After the words "This School", add the words "Received One-Year Short-Term Elementary School Education", and delete the words "Granted Graduation". Furthermore, this certificate does not need to be stamped by the county government. All departments are instructed to comply accordingly.

Ministry of Education Denies Participation in Sino-Japanese Elementary and Middle School Achievement Exhibition 167

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 17th) It was reported that the Ministry of Education had decided to collect the achievements of elementary and middle schools in preparation for participating in the Sino-Japanese Elementary and Middle School Achievement Exhibition to be held in Nagasaki, Japan. On the 17th, the person in charge of the relevant department of the Ministry of Education denied the matter to reporters. The Ministry has not prepared to participate in the exhibition, and the report is inaccurate.

Ministry of Education Orders Specialized Schools and Above to Report This Year's Graduates by a Specific Date 168

(Nanjing, 17th) The Ministry of Education issued an order to public and private specialized schools and above, stating that the list of students and subjects to be examined for graduation from all public and private specialized schools and above should be reported three months before the graduation examination. Although this has been ordered for two years, only a few schools have complied, and most have not reported on time, which is not right. Now that the deadline for reporting students to be examined for graduation in the 24th year of the Republic has passed, the previous order is reiterated. All public and registered private specialized schools and above must comply with the above regulations and report by a specific date. The Ministry will not review the qualifications of graduates, nor will it stamp their graduation certificates. All are instructed to comply.

News from Various Schools 180

Datong University: Datong University has been engaged in production and business since the year before last, starting with fish farming and tree planting as pilot projects. The school site is surrounded by streams for several miles, with clear and fertile water. Last spring, more than 300,000 fish fry were raised, and within a year, each grew to over a foot long. Last year, the Zhejiang Agricultural Experiment Station purchased many of them. Moreover, the school covers an area of more than 300 acres, and there is a lot of open space besides the buildings, so it is very suitable for planting tree seedlings. The current plantings include poplar, peach, willow, plum, osmanthus, paulownia, fir, and other trees, totaling no less than 100,000 plants. Due to proper cultivation, they are growing very rapidly. This month, the Shanghai Municipal Council purchased a large batch of poplars and willows from the school for use as roadside shade trees. It is heard that the school is also planning to decide on other production and business ventures, and the prospects are limitless.

Li devoted his life to the electrical industry and, feeling the need for electrical education among the Chinese people, founded the school. He had been struggling for four years to get to where it is today. Now that his ambition has not been realized, he has passed away, and all students of the Electrical Industry School should mourn him. Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (Part Two) (Zero) (Three) 182

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

The finale of one night's enjoyment was the Grand March of all the young people, starting with the pumpkin carriage, with Cinderella and the coachman transformed sitting in it, and the four great mice running and jumping in front.

As the children enjoyed this last prank, the adults sat in the living room watching, discussing the little ones with the interest of parents and friends.

"What are you thinking about there by yourself, with such a happy look on your face, Miss Shu?" Laurie asked, as he sat down next to her on a sofa.

She made room for him and replied with a smile, "Teddy, I was working on my summer plans and imagining the future of my boys, and I found it quite interesting."

"They will all become poets, painters, politicians, famous military strategists, or at least business leaders, I presume."

"No, I don't have as much hope as I used to. I would be content if they were honest people. But I must admit that I do harbor some hopes for the honor and greater future of a few of them. Xiao Qiao is not an ordinary child, I think he will develop into a truly good and great personality. The others can also achieve considerable success, I hope, especially the two boys I recently took in. Because after hearing Ned's performance tonight, I think he has talent."

Commercial News

Grain: Flour and Wheat Surge and Plummet 183

The flour market initially surged, but plummeted sharply in the afternoon. At the opening in the morning, although the quoted price of foreign wheat was still slightly lower by one cent, off-market participants were keen on speculation and actively buying, so the market atmosphere was also volatile. The highest for this month jumped to 3.322 yuan, for April to 3.3441 yuan, for June to 3.1195 yuan, for July to 3.115 yuan, and for August to 3.117 yuan, which were higher by three, four and five cents compared to the previous day. After three rounds, as the buyers slightly cleared out, it fell back by two or three cents. By the opening in the afternoon, after two rounds, the market remained tight due to the large buyers from outside the market. Afterwards, as the buying sentiment receded, although the factories continued to hedge, the momentum was hit. Each month fell by three, five and six cents compared to the highest in the morning. Looking at the current market atmosphere, it has entered such a high level. If the domestic new wheat harvest is good, it is necessary to guard against the reaction. However, the exchange's margin has been increased by one time to 500 yuan.

Closing Price on the 16th Closing Price on the 17th Comparison

March Term 3.3975 3.3875 Down 0.010

April Term 3.3850 3.3650 Down 0.020

June Term 3.1725 3.1325 Down 0.040

July Term 3.1000 3.0950 Down 0.005

August Term 3.1125 3.1150 Up 0.0025

At the opening of the wheat market, due to the alarming rise in prices in recent days, off-market buyers were universally excited. Therefore, after the opening, due to the activity of the buyers, the market improved step by step. Each month rose by five or six cents compared to the previous day. By the opening in the afternoon, it was initially calm. Afterwards, due to the return of bulls and the sharp reversal in the flour market, the market sentiment was very weak, and they were selling off. Compared to the highest price in the morning, it fell by a huge one cent. Compared to the previous day's closing price, it also fell by three to five cents. This kind of rise and fall is purely the result of market sentiment and has nothing to do with the facts. Currently, the high-quality wheat is being bid up by three to five cents. The medium-quality wheat remains the same. Kaihaizhou Shandong Yaowan wheat is 5.3 yuan, Hankou Che wheat is 5.25 yuan and 5.1125 yuan. The sub-quality wheat is 4.97 yuan. Fuxin bought 3,600 bags, and Shenda and Nafeng each bought 1,000 bags.

Rice Transactions Still Not Smooth 184

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, more than 30 ships arrived from various sources (nearly 7,000 shi of goods). The sales in this street are still sluggish, and the consumption is also not good, so the market conditions turned soft. The price of thick early japonica rice fell by five cents to one jiao. The price of thin indica rice is barely holding steady for the high-quality rice, and the medium-quality rice also continues to fall by nearly one jiao. According to statistics, Tianjin and Qingdao merchants bought more than 1,000 bags of thick japonica rice and more than 2,000 bags of thin indica rice. Duyangjian rice has no formal market, and sales are sluggish and falling by two or three jiao. The price of Yuan rice is fluctuating.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 18 or 19 ships arrived from various sources downriver. The market transactions are quiet. The price of white japonica rice is slightly lower by one jiao, and the price of early rice is slightly lower by nearly one jiao. The price of thin indica rice is slightly lower by seven or eight cents, and the price of Yinbian Yuan rice is slightly lower by six or seven cents. The sales of Yang Dufu Xian rice are weak, and the price is flat.

Indica Rice Sales Turn Sluggish 185

Yesterday, the Indica rice market continued to see arrivals from various ports, but the interior has long stopped buying, and the local consumption is also sluggish. Stockholders are even selling off, and the market conditions are quite weak and lifeless. However, Quanzhou merchants bought more than 300 bags of brown rice in small quantities, and Tianjin merchants also inquired about foreign rice, so Siamese rice bucked the trend and rose by four or five cents, with 500 bags sold. Although Indica rice did not fall, it still fell by about one jiao. A total of 1,000 bags of Gan rice, 62 bags of Anqing rice, 134 bags of Beijing brown rice, 400 bags of Hankou brown rice, and 200 bags of Taiwan indica rice were sold throughout the day. The market is still stable.

Oil Cakes Rebound and Fall – Slight Impact on Spot Market 186

The standard soybean cake markets fell sharply yesterday morning after the opening as various firms and merchants sold off along with factory hedging. All months saw flat prices, although Dalian telegrams had reported slight declines in both the cake and bean markets, the oil price briefly rose, which briefly turned the oil market in the morning. But in the afternoon, rumors were rampant, Dalian's telegrams returned lower, and the flour and wheat markets all shifted in unison, with continuous sales by factories and merchants and profit-taking by off-market bulls, resulting in a unanimous decline due to excessive gains in recent days and an immediate reaction to unexpected news. At closing, standard oil fell by three to four jiao, standard beans by one jiao, standard cakes by two to three cents, and foreign sesame by slightly more than two jiao.

The current spot soybean cake market has not been affected by the sharp decline in standard soybean cakes. The bean market was not good, but sales were inevitably reduced. Spring and Autumn

Snippets 203

— (Wu Wo)

The human heart is like the brilliance of the bright moon, eternally bright and pure; it is also like a pool of clear water, endlessly deep.

However, the human heart cannot be eternally bright and pure like the moonlight. It is like a pure white silver ingot, which turns into dark silver nitrate when it encounters nitric acid. Yet it will not become a valuable piece of black gold. It is also like a stone dropped into a pool of clear, bottomless water, "bang!" Splashes of water scatter everywhere, stirring up the silt at the bottom of the lake, immediately turning clarity into turbidity.

When a dark cloud comes, it obscures the brilliance of the bright moon, and the heavens and earth immediately turn dim. Therefore, when a person takes their bright heart and throws themselves into the world, brightness and purity will turn into turbidity. To go further, the world will easily form darkness!

The Ancestral Graves of the Feng and Shang Families 204

— Bright Moon

The art of geomancy has been passed down for a long time. People who are good at geomancy are generally called "geographers" or "feng shui masters." However, the relationship between geography, feng shui, and the fortunes of the living and the dead seems to be shrouded in incredible mystery.

It is said that Shang Qiyu (Zhen), one of the three chairmen from Shaoxing, has an ancestral grave in the Zhejiang Yidi in Baoding. This grave has been buried for decades and has not been repaired at all. Yet it still looks like a newly buried grave, with the soil color unchanged. In the spring and summer, it appears especially verdant and lovely. However, there are many graves in that Yidi, all connected to each other, but those that have fallen have fallen, and those that have collapsed have collapsed. None can remain unchanged for decades like the Shang family's ancestral grave. Therefore, a feng shui master said that this grave is located at the end of the earth's pulse, accumulating spiritual energy, and the future is promising. If this is the case, is the principle of feng shui really worth believing?

Feng Yuxiang also has an ancestral grave in Baoding. When it was exhumed and reburied in the south a few years ago, hot air steamed up from the soil, and wisteria vines were wrapped around the coffin, which was as new. When the vines were cut, white sap flowed out. According to those who know feng shui, this is a place with good feng shui, but it was ruined by Feng. It should be known that Feng Yuxiang has never liked superstition. After his ancestral grave was relocated, he did not encounter any disasters, and he is still an important figure in the party and the country. Then, so-called feng shui seems unbelievable.

Shop Number Five 205

— Wei Jing

Recently, our company transferred an accounting department director from the Hankou branch. Everyone secretly calls him "Shop Number Five." I found this very strange, and after inquiring, I learned that this so-called "Shop Number Five" has quite a history.

It happened seven years ago, when he was working as a shop assistant in a certain foreign firm. At that time, he was already in his thirties, earning only about twenty yuan a month. His family's life was naturally very difficult, so he pawned his sister in the red-light district. Coincidentally, the compradore in that foreign firm frequented prostitutes and fell in love at first sight, spending every evening there. At first, he did not know that his beloved was the shop assistant's sister from shop number five. After mingling for a while, the two even swore a blood oath, and the compradore paid to get her out of prostitution and made her a concubine, enjoying her exclusive favor. The shop assistant feared that his position would affect his sister's favor, so the siblings agreed to keep the secret from the compradore. But from then on, the shop assistant's family finances naturally improved.

After two months or so, something was bound to happen one day. The shop assistant went to his sister's house and met the compradore there. After questioning, the siblings could not hide it and had to confess everything. Unexpectedly, two days later, the shop assistant was promoted to "clerk." At the same time, the compradore ordered him to attend night school. Two years later, because of his hard work and study, his academics greatly improved. At the same time, because of his humble origins, he was despised by his colleagues and had a strong desire to leave. So the compradore recommended him to the company I now work for as an accountant. The compradore was a director of this company, and the compradore's son was also the associate manager, so he had a lot of influence.

A year later, the compradore's son took a fancy to his fifteen-year-old daughter, and he cleverly sent his daughter to him as an outside concubine. Then, he was dispatched to the Hankou branch as the accounting director. It was not until last autumn that he was transferred back to the head office as the accounting director, with a monthly salary of 250 yuan.

This accounting director is quite clever and capable, and he is also very loyal to his duties, so everyone does not have much ill feeling towards him. However, people who are familiar with his history always like to use the words "Shop Number Five" in private to represent his distinguished name.

Dog's Grave 206

— He Jiale

One or two months ago, a dog school was discovered in Shanghai, causing a sensation, because in China, dog protection has never received much attention. In Herrstel, USA, there have long been special facilities for dogs, including the construction of a magnificent cemetery in 1896, like a regular human cemetery. When a beloved dog of a certain family dies, they must buy a coffin. It is said that the most exquisite coffin costs 200 pounds. The most ordinary one also costs 10 to 20 pounds. After being sent to the cemetery for burial, a tombstone must be erected, stating the dog's name and the year of burial. Some even have "epitaphs" engraved on them.

In this Herrstel dog cemetery, there is a dog that died on the front lines during the European War, so a bronze statue was specially made and erected in the sky, looking down on everything. The words "War Dog Sacrificed for the Country" are engraved on the tombstone below. On every anniversary of its death, many people bring wreaths to pay tribute.

Some people say, "Better to be a dog in a peaceful time than a person in a chaotic world!" Their words show some envy for the animals in the land of gold.

Little Western Heaven 207

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 24. A Vulgar Man Chooses Love Over Money, A Determined and Strong Man Works in the Wilderness

Mr. Cheng was a little shorter and had no beard, but his yellow-black face and bald head were full of energy. Guo Zhuoran held Zhiqian's hand first and said, "County Chief Zhou said that Mr. Cheng is willing to join our group, and we are very welcome. We have decided to extend the trip by half a year." Zhiqian smiled and said, "I don't deserve that. My original plan to travel west only to Lanzhou was regrettable. I heard that to truly see the situation in the West, one must go beyond the Yumen Pass. So, I lingered in Xi'an, neither advancing nor retreating, just waiting for such an opportunity. Now that you two are organizing a tour group to the West, it perfectly suits my wishes." Guo Zhuoran waited for him to finish speaking before letting go of his hand. He sat to the side and nodded to Zhiqian, smiling, "We were very happy to hear from County Chief Zhou that Mr. Cheng had been to Gansu before. Because people who have not truly felt the joy of traveling cannot go there for the first time. Last time we went to Dihua via the Ningxia route, we only felt that it was just a corner of Xinjiang and could not be considered knowing Xinjiang. This time we are going west again, preparing to go to southern Xinjiang." Zhiqian was very happy, as if he couldn't express the joy in his heart. He just sat to the side, rubbing his hands together. Cheng Shigong smiled and said, "Seeing Mr. Cheng's situation, it is clear that he is one of our comrades. I heard that Mr. Cheng is willing to go to Qinghai, and we will definitely accompany you. I heard that there is also the Labrang tribe in the southwest corner of Gansu, and we also plan to visit them." Zhiqian said, "I met this tribe in Lanzhou. They wear purple cloth leather robes with sleeves that are more than three feet long, and the robes are only three feet long. They wear pointed hats, which look somewhat like the soap operas on the stage. A pair of high-waisted boots reach the knees. But they are very strong and can ride horses and shoot guns." Cheng Shigong smiled and said, "Speaking of the appearance of the people, Xinjiang is the most meaningful. When we see the Hui people, we mistakenly think they are Indians. When we see the southern Xinjiang Hui people, we mistakenly think they are Turks. In fact, they are our compatriots. As long as a person does not let down these two legs, there is a treasure trove of knowledge everywhere in the universe. We are only afraid that we ourselves are unwilling to go and find it." Zhiqian clapped his legs and laughed, "Don't say anything else, I dare not be arrogant, but speaking of these two legs, they are quite strong." (417)

Special Feature in this Publication

Ferry Crossing on the Whangpoo 208

— Huang Kewei

Like fallen leaves in autumn, on the turbid currents of the Whangpoo River, huge warships and merchant vessels move up and down, piece by piece, quietly drifting.

Every day, from morning to night, braving the misty haze, accompanied by the loud steam whistles, gently rocking their creaky wooden awnings, carrying boats full of people, from Pudong to Puxi, from Puxi to Pudong, tirelessly shuttling back and forth to earn a meager fare.

They live on the water; the Whangpoo River is so familiar and dear to them!

Perhaps driven by curiosity, one day, on the way back from a friend's house, I deliberately took a small sampan to Puxi for a fresh and slightly thrilling experience.

It was early spring afternoon, and the bright sun painted a layer of gold on the river water. Tiny waves shimmered brilliantly, and droplets splashed on the oars like many tiny, transparent pearls.

On this vast river, sitting in such a small ferry, one truly feels so small, while the river surface feels even more expansive! When a steamboat passes by, the boat violently pitches, shaking up and down, giving one's nerves a little jolt of terror.

The boatman was an elderly man in his fifties. Although his face was etched with many wrinkles from the trials of life, making him look very old, he was full of energy, and rowing was very vigorous. During this short several-minute voyage, while admiring the scenery of Puxi, I casually asked him:

"How much money can you make in a day?"

"At most, only a little over a thousand cash; sometimes, I can't even earn a few hundred!"

His tone of voice concealed a long sigh, but he didn't utter it, only expressing his inner distress with a bitter smile!

A small steamer belonging to the Taikoo Dockyard & Engineering Company was steaming majestically towards us from the opposite direction, packed with people. He suddenly said softly: "Ships like these company boats are fast and stable, and they don't cost money, so naturally more people ride them. They've taken a big chunk of our business!"

At this moment, the boat shook violently again. I stared wistfully at the company boats crowded with passengers, deeply feeling that these small ferries are struggling on the turbulent river!

Travel Musings

A Record of Visiting Plum Blossoms in the Snow 209

— Xiafei

Plum blossoms are originally nothing rare in my hometown of Xishan, Dongting Lake, because our houses are almost built in plum groves. As long as you open the door and look up, you see the pure white and lovely plum blossoms; sometimes, plum groves stretch continuously for one or two miles, and as we walk along the paths under the trees, we can't even see a patch of sky. But this year when I returned home, although it was the season for viewing plum blossoms, because of the cold weather, the plum blossoms everywhere were still only budding, and wouldn't seem likely to bloom for another ten days or half a month.

A week later, the weather suddenly turned much colder, so cold that it felt almost like the depths of winter; and from the evening, goose feather-like snowflakes began to fall from the sky, without stopping for the entire night. When I opened the door the first morning and looked out, I saw that the roofs, trees, and ground were all covered with a thick layer of white snow. Opening my eyes, I felt as if I were in a world of powdered makeup and jade construction. Even the Four Dragon Mountain, Chicken Cage Mountain in front, the Linwu Mountain below, the Eight Cannon Ridge above, and the Mao Gong Wu behind were all draped in white robes.

In such a magnificent and beautiful scene, the nearby plum blossoms were still sound asleep, so I had to abandon the close and seek the distant, and go to Baoshan to visit plum blossoms in the snow. Because the location there faces the sun, the plum blossoms on Chaoyang Mountain usually bloom a month earlier.

Xiong and I set off. In the afternoon, with a faint sunlight shining on the earth, we walked onto Changshan Road, following the traces of the monks' straw sandals, passed through the Hongshan Gate, crossed Beiyin Mountain, and arrived at the Chaoyang Stream.

As I walked among the plum trees, I accidentally touched a branch, and snowflakes and plum petals fell rustling onto my hair and clothes; but I couldn't bear to brush away these accumulated snow and plum petals, wanting them to stay on my hairline and on my sleeves forever.

Walking on the snow in leather shoes was very easy to slip. Xiong slipped and fell on the hillside while stepping over a large stone. Because I had learned from his mistake, I walked particularly carefully, always grabbing onto the small tree trunks with each step.

In Chaoyang Gully, the streams flowed gurgling, the water was clear and lovely, and the small round stones at the bottom of the gully were all clearly visible. The verdant pine forest on the hillside sent forth the majestic sound of the pine waves, and the fragrance of some wildflowers in the mountains, although buried under the snow, still drifted in bursts.

Xiong leaned against an old plum tree and said to me, "It's a pity we didn't bring a camera. Otherwise, we could have taken some pictures of the snow scene and plum blossoms to take back as a memento!"

At that time, I was walking around the plum grove, gazing at the silver-white plum blossoms, and my heart felt incredibly carefree, as if cleansed of all dust. Although it was the chill of early spring, with the northwest wind sweeping across, I finally climbed up that not-very-high foothill, overlooking the plum blossoms in all directions; I found a plum tree with a unique trunk and horizontal branches, and sat down on a rock, silently gazing up at the treetop. Infinite melancholy and emotion welled up! Thinking that for the sake of life, I had been wandering for half my life, falling into obscurity for a decade, but every time I returned, the mountains and rivers were still the same, while people had changed repeatedly, and the old friends and companions of the past were no longer to be found. Only this plum grove could allow me to reminisce about the remnants of my childhood; but youth had passed, and my state of mind was no longer the same. It was only making future generations feel sentimental!

"Separated from the mortal world by three thousand miles, this heavenly fairy-like beauty, this noble and unsullied character, how lovely it is!" Just as I was lost in thought, I was awakened by a few lines of poetic praise from Xiong.

Acknowledgment: The Healthy World Monthly, published by the Kangjian Shijie Society at No. 214, Lane 2, Tongfu Road in this city, has now published its fifth issue. The content is quite wonderful, and it makes great efforts to impart health knowledge. The pre-paid price for twelve issues domestically, including postage, is only fifty cents in national currency. We received two complimentary copies yesterday, and hereby acknowledge our thanks and introduce it to our readers.
